## F
## by Ruth Kinna

In March  Ptr Kropotkin agrd to giv si lcturs to William Morris’s Socialist Socity in Hammrsmith, London. Lalling th sris “Social Evolution,” h plannd to plor “th grounds” o socialism.1 As it turnd out, h nvr dlivrd th talks, ut th titl and timing, just a yar or h pulishd his rst ssay on mutual aid, hint at th contnt. H l a iggr clu whn h told Morris’s daughtr May that h had n working on th sris during his rcnt tour o Scotland. According to local prss rports, on o th issus on Kropotkin’s mind was th asiility o socialism. Prhaps rashly, givn that on critic had dismissd his socialism as a util, dangrous schm to “rach Arcady through anarchy,” h told an Ardn mting that too many workrs attractd to socialism still livd it impractical.2 Th account o social volution h outlind in Mutual Aid: A Factor of Evolution was a rspons to this scpticism and it has sinc com his most clratd rutation.
       Th concpt o mutual aid is outlind in ight ssays. Th rst,
“Mutual Aid among Animals,” was pulishd in  in th journal The Nineteenth Century. By , Kropotkin had compltd th othrs. Th rsulting ook was pulishd in , ut Kropotkin continud to dvlop th concpt, notaly in Anarchism: Its Philosophy and Ideal (); The State: Its Historic Role (); and Modern Science and Anarchism (). Som thirty yars ar starting his invstigations, h issud his nal, incomplt statmnt, posthumously pulishd as Ethics, Origin and Development (). Each nw itration rought out a difrnt act o th concpt: th rprssiv charactr o th modrn Europan stat, th impulss driving mplary haviours, th asis o moral action, th principl o justic that morality dscrid, and th structural mchanisms or its acculturation. Th common thrad tying ths strands togthr was Kropotkin’s viw that socialism tappd an innat tndncy to cooprat common to all living things. Socialism was nithr th utopists’ candy mountain nor th salvationists’ pi in th sky. It was a potntial altrnativ. Th thrust o
Kropotkin’s argumnt was that isting disciplinary, ploitativ ordrs had institutionalizd comptition and individual struggl, wrongly pr- snting this haviour as natural. Against this, th thory o mutual aid dmonstratd that thr was nothing invital, prordaind, much lss moral or good aout ths arrangmnts. Natur was plastic and thr- or mallal to orcs capal o uilding convivial, lirtarian social systms.
      Mutual Aid lnds itsl to multipl intrprtations. This is partly
caus Kropotkin thorisd it y intrvning in a longstanding dat aout th social and thical implications o Charls Darwin’s Origin of Species. In doing so, h nthusiastically adoptd Victorian intrdisciplinary convntions, rading across th arts and scincs to marshal vidnc rom zoology, history, art and nwr disciplins, notaly sociology, thnography and anthropology, which wr qually multiactd.3 Ironically, as Kropotkin dcrid spcialisation, th synthtic quality o Mutual Aid has sinc nald tams o scholars in th humanitis and natural and social scincs to ring thir spcial disciplinary prspctivs to ar on it. Sinc th pulication o Danil P. Tods’s pivotal ssay in , Mutual Aid is now commonly situatd in a roadr ody o Russian volutionary thought.4 But th divrsity o th litratur on it and th rang o its concptual rsonancs is vast.5 In th othr part, Kropotkin dvlopd critical Russian volutionary iology to show how his account o Darwinian thory posd th aws in compting li systms. Kropotkin livd th principl o mutual aid scotchd Christian moralising, utilitarianism, Marist matrialism and Nitzschan individualism.6 His naturalistic, “scintic” dnc o anarchism thus lnds itsl to comparison with all ths standpoints, whil also nourishing critics intrstd in uncovring anarchism’s ssntialist rrors.7
Mutual Aid and Evolutionary Theory Kropotkin idntid Thomas Huly, grandathr o th novlist and philosophr Aldous Huly and Darwin’s “ulldog,” as th lading proponnt o th social Darwinist viw that natur was st dscrid as a comptitiv ght or individual advantag. Th viw, popularisd y Hrrt Spncr, was a sociological rndring o Darwin’s account o natural slction, th mchanism plaining th inhritanc o chanc variations fctiv or survival. Rcasting Darwin’s “struggl or istnc” as th “survival o th ttst,” th social Darwinists conatd struggl with comptition and appald to “natur” to stalish th “goodnss” o individualistic, com- ativ social systms, notaly laissz-air liralism.
       Kropotkin’s viw, sinc partially validatd y th lading volutionary iologist Stphn Jay Gould, was that Darwin had himsl opnd th
door to Spncr’s sociological rworking o his thsis y accpting Thomas Malthus’s calculations aout population incrass outstripping ood supplis to uild an assumption o scarcity into his ramwork.8 This narrowd th maning o struggl to “rivalry,” ovrshadowing th rich “mtaphorical” concption Darwin had invokd in th Origin. Undrstood as a mtaphor, “struggl” involvd cological and spcis’ intrdpndnc and it rcognisd that individuals struggld collctivly to ovrcom nvironmntal hardships and protct thir ofspring. Th priority which Darwin accordd to Malthus—wrongly in Kropotkin’s viw—downplayd ths mods o action. Th rsult was to distract attntion rom th advantags that individuals drivd rom coopration. Mutual aid was intndd to corrct this ias y rstoring th missing actor o volution to Darwin’s account. Somtims drawing on osrvations h had mad during his pditions in Siria in th s and ’s, Kropotkin usd th rst two chaptrs o th ook, “Mutual Aid among Animals,” to argu that (i) spcis struggl against “advrs circumstancs o climat, or against vicious nmis,” (ii) that “ral comptition and struggl” within spcis is rar, (iii) that “trmination” only occurs as a rsult o human action, not intrspcis comptition, and (iv) that migrations or nvironmntal changs account or inhritd variations.9
       Soon ar th ook’s pulication, Kropotkin prssd this argumnt.
In a scond st o ssays or The Nineteenth Century, h dtachd Malthus rom Darwin’s work, fctivly lvating th mtaphorical ovr th narrow concption o struggl.10 Stopping short o radicating natural slction rom Darwin’s work altogthr, h argud that th dirct impact o th nvironmnt plaind th inhritanc o acquird charactristics qually wll. In addition, th wight o modrn scinc inclind towards this viw. Whn Kropotkin invstigatd th volution o Darwin’s rsarch, h nally wrot Malthus out. It turnd out that Darwin had also avourd th dirct impact o th nvironmnt ovr natural sction ut had unortunatly n unal ully to rvis his pulishd work or h did. According to Kropotkin, natural slction had n a working hypothsis, not Darwin’s sttld viw. Driving a wdg twn Darwin and his “vulgarisrs” in , Kropotkin rturnd to his main thm. aout th ncssity o comptition to th kni twn all th individuals o a givn spcis or volving nw spcis, opns th way or a quit di- rnt comprhnsion o th struggl or li, and o Natur altogthr.”12

      Adopting discourss o colonialism, Kropotkin turnd dominant
civilization narrativs on thir had. His analysis is conttualisd, not astract. It difrs markdly rom Jan-Jacqus Roussau’s modlling o th nol savag in th stat o natur.      Kropotkin’s argumnt that coopration is a suprior principl or

Evolution and Revolution Rvolutionary chang was th natural countrpart to Kropotkin’s volutionary social thory. Kropotkin’s proposals, outlind in The Conquest of Bread and Fields, Factories and Workshops, wr to dscal and drat. H imagind th commun as th asic social unit with a nw political conomy o nds asd on th aolition o laour divisions, wag systms and intrnational trad supportd y th intgration o agricultur and industry in localitis. Mutual aid was th mans and th ojct o this transormation. Anarchist communism was a modl or “consnsus” which rquird coopration to ring it into ing.

to th importanc o th organizational aspcts o coopration. and raids, trial wars, glutton kings, dciving witchs and prists, slav- huntrs, and th lik” th “nuclus o mutual-aid institutions, haits and customs, growing up in th tri and th villag community, rmains.”49 Colonisd popls did not rquir prparation or sl-govrnmnt. Thy did not nd th chis who had n mpowrd y colonisrs to rul thm or th rising class o local ducatd lits who sought to oust oth to implmnt dirct rul.
      Kropotkin was similarly nthusd y th nw orms o coopration
and mutual aid vstd in a plthora o cultural associations and, spcially, socialist organisations and actions: syndicats, trad unions, striks, political movmnts, nwspaprs.       Rvolution ntaild protcting, nurturing and tnding ths multi-
arious mutual aid organisations to acilitat th haitual prssion o th psychology. As a gloal rcis, th projct inscapaly hightnd divrsity.       In Mutual Aid Kropotkin usd his “anarchizd” volutionary thory
to attack advocats o stat ordr or “suordination.” Whil this includd laissz-air lirals and consrvativs o all strips, h promotd his concpt o rvolution to highlight th shortcomings o currnts within socialist and anarchist movmnts. In th s Mikhail Bakunin had idntid rpulicans and Marists as advocats o political thology, as antagonistic to anarchy as any asolutist or clric. Kropotkin ollowd suit ut idntid Nitzschans and Marists and th lading advocats o comptition and “suordination” lial to drail th socialist caus rom within. also undrmind th cohsion o th workrs’ associations. In doing so, thy dstroyd grassroots initiativs to considr conomic, political, and moral qustions “prcursory” to rvolutionary transormation.50 Writing to Alandr Brkman in , h rmarkd, “It is th Masss which mak th Rvolutions—not th Individuals.” Osrving that Europan workrs had “aandond” groups ar thy had n “invadd y all sorts o middl class tramps,” h addd, “vn th rally rvolutionary mindd individuals, i thy rmain isolatd, turn towards this Individualist Anarchism o th ourgois which is nothing ut th picuran let it go o th Economists, spicd with a w ‘trric’ phrass o Nihilism.” This was “ood to rightn th Philistins” and st l to “th Nitzsch’ists . . . Brnard Shaw’ists, and all th similar arch-Philistin’ists.’”51
     I th Nitzschans’ loy dismissal o organization ndangrd th

          C G
Through sharing knowledge, resources, and good company, crafting guilds enable individuals to develop their skills. Individuals are able to expand their craft through collective learning and skill sharing, nding joy in creating together. In the example of quilting guilds, often works produced
     are gifted to people in hospice care, exiting
prisons, or accessing domestic violence shelters.

##  A

Struggle for existence.—Mutual aid—a law of Nature and chief factor of progressive evolution.—Invertebrates.—Ants and bees.—Birds: Hunting and shing associations.—Sociability.—Mutual protection among small birds.—Cranes; parrots.

      In that immns division o th animal kingdom which modis mor

kingdom. In act, th ant thrivs without having any o th “protctiv” aturs which cannot  dispnsd with y animals living an isolatd li. In act, th whit-taild agl—on o th ravst and st huntrs—is a grgarious ird altogthr, and Brhm says that whn kpt in captivity it vry soon contracts an attachmnt to its kprs.
     Sociaility is a common atur with vry many othr irds o pry.
Th Brazilian kit, on o th most “impudnt” rors, is nvrthlss a most social ird. Its hunting associations hav n dscrid y Darwin and othr naturalists, and it is a act that whn it has sizd upon a pry which is too ig, it calls togthr v or si rinds to carry it away. Ar
a usy day, whn ths kits rtir or thir night-rst to a tr or to th ushs, thy always gathr in ands, somtims coming togthr rom distancs o tn or mor mils, and thy on ar joind y svral othr vulturs, spcially th prcnoptrs, “thir tru rinds,” D’Origny says. Thy st of ying, all at onc, in a quit straight lin, towards som dtrmind point, and, having rachd it, immdiatly rturnd ovr th sam lin, to rpat th sam ight.15
     To tak ights in ocks or th mr plasur o th ight, is quit

     It would  quit impossil to numrat hr th various hunting
associations o irds; ut th shing associations o th plicans ar crtainly worthy o notic or th rmarkal ordr and intllignc displayd y ths clumsy irds. divid into two partis, ach o which draws up on a hal-circl, and oth paddl to mt ach othr, just as i two partis o mn dragging two long nts should advanc to captur all sh takn twn th nts whn oth partis com to mt.      Hunting and ding in common is so much th hait in th athrd
world that mor quotations hardly would  ndul: it must  considrd as an stalishd act. As to th orc drivd rom such associations, it is sl-vidnt. Evn agls—vn th powrul and trril ootd agl, and th martial agl, which is strong nough to carry away a har or a young antlop in its claws—ar complld to aandon thir pry to ands o thos ggars th kits, which giv th agl a rgular chas as soon as thy s it in possssion o a good pry. Th kits will also giv chas to th swi shing-hawk and ro it o th sh it has capturd; ut no on vr saw th kits ghting togthr or th possssion o th pry so stoln. soon as it cam nar to thir aods, spcially at nsting-tim.19 Th littl, ut trmly swi lapwings (Vanellus cristatus) oldly attack th irds o pry. “To s thm attacking a uzzard, a kit, a crow, or an agl, is on o th most amusing spctacls. On ls that thy ar sur o victory, and on ss th angr o th ird o pry. In such circumstancs thy prctly support on anothr, and thir courag grows with thir numrs.20 Th lapwing has wll mritd th nam o a “good mothr” which th Grks gav to it, or it nvr ails to protct othr aquatic irds rom th attacks o thir nmis. But vn th littl whit wagtails (Motacilla alba), whom w wll know in our gardns and whos whol lngth hardly attains ight inchs, compl th sparrow-hawk to aandon its hunt. “I on admird thir courag and agility,” th old Brhm wrot, “and I am prsuadd that th alcon alon is capal o capturing any o thm. . . .       What an immns difrnc twn th orc o a kit, a uzzard or
a hawk, and such small irds as th madow-wagtail; and yt ths littl irds, y thir common action and courag, prov suprior to th powr- ully wingd and armd rors! In Europ, th wagtails not only chas th irds o pry which might  dangrous to thm, ut thy chas also th shing-hawk “rathr or un than or doing it any harm”; whil in India, according to Dr. Jrdon’s tstimony, th jackdaws chas th govinda-kit “or simpl mattr o amusmnt.” Princ Wid saw th Brazilian agl urubitinga surroundd y numrlss ocks o toucans and cassiqus (a ird narly akin to our rook), which mockd it. “Th agl,” h adds, “usually supports ths insults vry quitly, ut rom tim to tim it will catch on o ths mockrs.” In all such cass th littl irds, though vry much inrior in orc to th ird o pry, prov suprior to it y thir common action.21
       Howvr, th most striking fcts o common li or th scurity
o th individual, or its njoymnt o li, and or th dvlopmnt o its intllctual capacitis, ar sn in two grat amilis o irds, th crans and th parrots. Th crans ar trmly social and liv in most cllnt rlations, not only with thir congnrs, ut also with most aquatic irds. Thir prudnc is rally astonishing, so also thir intllignc; thy grasp th nw conditions in a momnt, and act accordingly. Thir sntris always
kp watch around a ock which is ding or rsting, and th huntrs know wll how dicult it is to approach thm.     C C
By sharing the responsibilities and joys involved in raising the very young, caretaking is distributed and burdens lessened. Pregnant people receive
     information and advocacy and have their
physical and emotional needs addressed by birth care workers. New parents receive delivery of essential items such as breast milk or healthy foods. Collectives provide support for caretakers
       and parents through no-cost childcare.
  M A  A ()
Migrations of birds.—Breeding associations.—Autumn societies.—Mammals: small number of unsociable species.—Hunting associations of wolves, lions, etc.— Societies of rodents; of ruminants; of monkeys.—Mutual aid in the struggle for life.—Darwin’s arguments to prove the struggle for life within the species.— Natural checks to over-multiplication.—Supposed extermination of intermediate links.—Elimination of competition in Nature.

Hr you hav th dominativ swans; thr, th trmly social kittiwak-gulls, among whom quarrls ar rar and short; th prpossssing polar guillmots, which continually carss ach othr; th goist sh-goos, who has rpudiatd th orphans o a killd comrad; and, y hr sid, anothr mal who adopts any on’s orphans, and now paddls surroundd y y or sity youngstrs, whom sh conducts and cars or as i thy all wr hr own rd. Natur is varity itsl, ofring all possil varitis o charactrs, rom th asst to th highst: and that is why sh cannot  dpictd y any swping assrtion.      Coming togthr at nsting-tim is so common with most irds that

     Not long ago th small strams o Northrn Amrica and Northrn

     Association and mutual aid ar th rul with mammals. W nd social

It is wll known, in act, that wolvs gathr in packs or hunting, and Tschudi l an cllnt dscription o how thy draw up in a hal-circl, surround a cow which is grazing on a mountain slop, and thn, suddnly apparing with a loud arking, mak it roll in th ayss.12 Auduon, in th thirtis, also saw th Larador wolvs hunting in packs, and on pack ollowing a man to his cain, and killing th dogs. During svr wintrs th packs o wolvs grow so numrous as to com a dangr or human sttlmnts, as was th cas in Franc som v-and- orty yars ago. th risk o ing surroundd y th horss and killd y thir hoos. Th prairi-wolvs (Canis latrans) ar known to associat in ands o rom twnty to thirty individuals whn thy chas a ufalo occasionally sparatd rom its hrd.13 Jackals, which ar most couragous and may  considrd as on o th most intllignt rprsntativs o th dog tri, always hunt in packs; thus unitd, thy hav no ar o th iggr carnivors.14 As to th wild dogs o Asia (th Kholzuns, or Dholes), Williamson saw thir larg packs attacking all largr animals sav lphants and rhinoc- ross, and ovrpowring ars and tigrs. Most o our irds slowly mov southwards as th wintr coms, or gathr in numrlss socitis and undrtak long journys—and thus avoid comptition.      “Don’t compt!—comptition is always injurious to th spcis, and
you hav plnty o rsourcs to avoid it!” That is th tendency o natur, not always ralizd in ull, ut always prsnt. That is th watchword which coms to us rom th ush, th orst, th rivr, th ocan. “Thror
comin—practic mutual aid!            F A 
             D
By disrespecting the property claims of stores to their dumpsters and through pooling resources, people can provide food security and shared community. Some groups will identify unique community needs, such as meals for pregnant or ill people, and specialize their cooking and distribution to ll those needs and ensure that everyone has access to hot meals.

##  S

spoil without quarrlling; that thy nvr aandond thir woundd, and displayd strong afction to thir comrads. Lichtnstin has a most touching story aout a Bushman, narly drownd in a rivr, who was rscud y his companions.     thy vry sldom at mmrs o thir own tri (whn immolatd on
    rligious principls, I suppos); thy at strangrs only. Th parnts
    lov thir childrn, play with thm, and pt thm. Inanticid mts
    with common approval. Old popl ar vry wll tratd, nvr put
    to dath. No rligion, no idols, only a ar o dath. Polygamous marriag, quarrls arising within th tri ar sttld y mans o duls
    ought with woodn swords and shilds. No slavs; no cultur o
    any kind; no pottry; no drss, sav an apron somtims worn y

For th Papuas, closly akin to th aov, w hav th tstimony o G.L. Bink, who stayd in Nw Guina, chiy in Glwink Bay, rom  to . Hr is th ssnc o his answrs to th sam qustionr:21
    Thy ar social and chrul; thy laugh vry much. Rathr timid
    than couragous. Frindship is rlativly strong among prsons
    longing to difrnt tris, and still strongr within th tri. A
    rind will on pay th dt o his rind, th stipulation ing that
    th lattr will rpay it without intrst to th childrn o th lndr.
    Thy tak car o th ill and th old; old popl ar nvr aandond,

    long tim. War prisonrs ar somtims atn. Th childrn ar vry
    much pttd and lovd. Old and l war prisonrs ar killd, th
    othrs ar sold as slavs. Thy hav no rligion, no gods, no idols, no
    authority o any dscription; th oldst man in th amily is th judg.
    In cass o adultry a n is paid, and part o it gos to th negoria
    (th community). Th soil is kpt in common, ut th crop longs to

    ar rturnd.22 Thy ar had-huntrs, and in so doing thy proscut
    lood rvng. “Somtims,” Finsch says, “th afair is rrrd to th
    Rajah o Namotott, who trminats it y imposing a n.”
    Whn wll tratd, th Papuas ar vry kind. Miklukho-Maclay landd
on th astrn coast o Nw Guina, ollowd y on singl man, stayd or two yars among tris rportd to  cannials, and l thm with rgrt; h rturnd again to stay on yar mor among thm, and nvr had h any conict to complain o. Tru that his rul was never—undr no prtt whatvr—to say anything which was not truth, nor mak any promis which h could not kp. Ths poor craturs, who vn do not know how to otain r, and carully maintain it in thir huts, liv undr thir primitiv communism, without any chis; and within thir villags thy hav no quarrls worth spaking o. Thy work in common, just nough
to gt th ood o th day; thy rar thir childrn in common; and in th vnings thy drss thmslvs as coquttishly as thy can, and danc. Lik all savags, thy ar ond o dancing. Each villag has its barla, or balai—th “long hous,” “longu maison,” or “grand maison”—or th unmarrid mn, or social gathrings, and or th discussion o common afairs—again a trait which is common to most inhaitants o th Pacic Islands, th Eskimos, th Rd Indians, and so on. Whol groups o villags ar on rindly trms, and visit ach othr en bloc.
      Unhappily, uds ar not uncommon—not in consqunc o
“Ovrstocking o th ara,” or “kn comptition,” and lik invntions o a mrcantil cntury, ut chiy in consqunc o suprstition. As soon as any on alls ill, his rinds and rlativs com togthr, and dliratly discuss who might  th caus o th illnss. All possil nmis ar considrd, vry on consss o his own ptty quarrls, and nally th ral caus is discovrd.       Many striking pags could  writtn aout th harmony which pr-
vails in th villags o th Polynsian inhaitants o th Pacic Islands. But thy long to a mor advancd stag o civilization. So w shall now tak our illustrations rom th ar north. I must mntion, howvr, or laving th Southrn Hmisphr, that vn th Fugians, whos rputation has n so ad, appar undr a much ttr light sinc thy gin to  ttr known. A w Frnch missionaris who stay among thm “know o no act o malvolnc to complain o.” In thir clans, consisting o rom  to  souls, thy practic th sam primitiv communism as th Papuas; thy shar vrything in common, and trat thir old popl vry wll. Pac prvails among ths tris.24
      With th Eskimos and thir narst congnrs, th Thlinkts, th
Koloshs, and th Alouts, w nd on o th narst illustrations o what man may hav n during th glacial ag. Thir implmnts hardly difr rom thos o palaolithic man, and som o thir tris do not yt know shing: thy simply spar th sh with a kind o harpoon.25 Thy know th us o iron, ut thy rciv it rom th Europans, or nd it on wrckd ships. Thir social organization is o a vry primitiv kind, though thy alrady hav mrgd rom th stag o “communal marriag,” vn undr th gntil rstrictions. Thy liv in amilis, ut th amily onds
ar on rokn; husands and wivs ar on changd.26 Th amilis, howvr, rmain unitd in clans, and how could it  othrwis? How could thy sustain th hard struggl or li unlss y closly comining thir orcs? So thy do, and th trial onds ar closst whr th struggl or li is hardst, namly, in North-East Grnland. Th “long hous” is thir usual dwlling, and svral amilis lodg in it, sparatd rom ach othr y small partitions o raggd urs, with a common passag in th ront. Somtims th hous has th shap o a cross, and in such cas a common r is kpt in th cntr. Th Grman Epdition which spnt a wintr clos y on o thos “long houss” could ascrtain that “no quarrl disturd th pac, no disput aros aout th us o this narrow spac” throughout th long wintr. “Scolding, or vn unkind words, ar considrd as a misdmanour, i not producd undr th lgal orm o procss, namly, th ninth-song.”27 Clos cohaitation and clos intrdpndnc ar sucint or maintaining cntury ar cntury that dp rspct or th intrsts o th community which is charactristic o Eskimo li. Evn in th largr communitis o Eskimos, “pulic opinion ormd th ral judgmnt-sat, th gnral punishmnt consisting in th ofndrs ing shamd in th ys o th popl.”28
      Eskimo li is asd upon communism. What is otaind y hunting
and shing longs to th clan. But in svral tris, spcially in th Wst, undr th inunc o th Dans, privat proprty pntrats into thir institutions. Howvr, thy hav an original mans or oviating th inconvnincs arising rom a prsonal accumulation o walth which would soon dstroy thir trial unity. Whn a man has grown rich, h convoks th olk o his clan to a grat stival, and, ar much ating, distriuts among thm all his ortun. On th Yukon rivr, Dall saw an Alout amily distriuting in this way tn guns, tn ull ur drsss,  strings o ads, numrous lankts, tn wol urs,  avrs, and  zilins. Ar that thy took of thir stival drsss, gav thm away, and, putting on old raggd urs, addrssd a w words to thir kinsolk, saying that though thy ar now poorr than any on o thm, thy hav won thir rindship.29 Lik distriutions o walth appar to  a rgular hait with th Eskimos, and to tak plac at a crtain sason, ar an hiition o all that has n otaind during th yar.30 In my opinion ths distriutions rval a vry old institution, contmporanous with th rst apparition o prsonal walth; thy must hav n a mans or r-stalishing quality among th mmrs o th clan, ar it had n disturd y th nrichmnt o th w. Th priodical rdistriution o land and th priodical aandonmnt o all dts which took plac in historical tims with so many difrnt racs
(Smits, Aryans, tc.), must hav n a survival o that old custom. And th hait o ithr urying with th dad, or dstroying upon his grav, all that longd to him prsonally—a hait which w nd among all primitiv racs—must hav had th sam origin. In act, whil vrything that longs personally to th dad is urnt or rokn upon his grav, nothing is dstroyd o what longd to him in common with th tri, such as oats, or th communal implmnts o shing. Th dstruction ars upon prsonal proprty alon. At a latr poch this hait coms a rligious crmony. It rcivs a mystical intrprtation, and is imposd y rligion, whn pulic opinion alon provs incapal o norcing its gnral osrvanc. And, nally, it is sustitutd y ithr urning simpl modls o th dad man’s proprty (as in China), or y simply carrying his proprty to th grav and taking it ack to his hous ar th urial crmony is ovr—a hait which still prvails with th Europans as rgards swords, crosss, and othr marks o pulic distinction.31
     Th high standard o th trial morality o th Eskimos has on n
mntiond in gnral litratur. Nvrthlss th ollowing rmarks upon th mannrs o th Alouts—narly akin to th Eskimos—will ttr illustrat savag morality as a whol. Thy wr writtn, ar a tn yars’ stay among th Alouts, y a most rmarkal man—th Russian missionary, Vniaminof. I sum thm up, mostly in his own words:
    Enduraility is thir chi atur. It is simply colossal. Not only do
    thy ath vry morning in th rozn sa, and stand nakd on th

    work on insucint ood, surpasss all that can  imagind. During
    a protractd scarcity o ood, th Alout cars rst or his childrn;
    h givs thm all h has, and himsl asts. Thy ar not inclind to
    staling; that was rmarkd vn y th rst Russian immigrants. Not
    that thy nvr stal; vry Alout would conss having somtim
    stoln somthing, ut it is always a tri; th whol is so childish. Th
    attachmnt o th parnts to thir childrn is touching, though it is
    nvr prssd in words or pttings. Th Alout is with diculty
    movd to mak a promis, ut onc h has mad it h will kp it
    whatvr may happn. (An Alout mad Vniaminof a gi o drid
    sh, ut it was orgottn on th ach in th hurry o th dpartur.
    H took it hom. Th nt occasion to snd it to th missionary was
    in January; and in Novmr and Dcmr thr was a grat scarcity
     o ood in th Alout ncampmnt. But th sh was nvr touchd
    y th starving popl, and in January it was snt to its dstination.)
    Thir cod o morality is oth varid and svr. It is considrd
    shamul to  araid o unavoidal dath; to ask pardon rom an
    nmy; to di without vr having killd an nmy; to  convictd
    o staling; to capsiz a oat in th harour; to  araid o going to
    sa in stormy wathr. to  th rst in a party on a long journy
    to com an invalid in cas o scarcity o ood; to show grdinss
    whn spoil is dividd, in which cas vry on givs his own part to
    th grdy man to sham him; to divulg a pulic scrt to his wi;
    ing two prsons on a hunting pdition, not to ofr th st gam
    to th partnr; to oast o his own dds, spcially o invntd ons;
    to scold any on in scorn. Also to g; to pt his wi in othr popl’s

    woman it is a sham not to know swing, dancing and all kinds o
    woman’s work; to pt hr husand and childrn, or vn to spak to

Such is Alout morality, which might also  urthr illustratd y thir tals and lgnds. Lt m also add that whn Vniaminof wrot (in ) on murdr only had n committd sinc th last cntury in a population o , popl, and that among , Alouts not on singl common law ofnc had n known or orty yars. This will not sm strang i w rmark that scolding, scorning, and th us o rough words ar asolutly unknown in Alout li. Evn thir childrn nvr ght, and nvr aus ach othr in words. All thy may say is, “Your mothr dos not know swing,” or “Your athr is lind o on y.”33
     Many aturs o savag li rmain, howvr, a puzzl to Europans.
Th high dvlopmnt o trial solidarity and th good lings with which primitiv olk ar animatd towards ach othr, could  illustratd y any amount o rlial tstimony. And yt it is not th lss crtain that thos sam savags practic inanticid; that in som cass thy aandon thir old popl, and that thy lindly oy th ruls o lood rvng. W must thn plain th coistnc o acts which, to th Europan mind, sm so contradictory at th rst sight. I hav just mntiond how th Alout athr starvs or days and wks, and givs vrything atal to his child; and how th Bushman mothr coms a slav to ollow hr child; and I might ll pags with illustrations o th rally tender rlations isting among th savags and thir childrn. Travllrs continually mntion thm incidntally. Hr you rad aout th ond lov o a mothr; thr you s a athr wildly running through th orst and carrying upon his shouldrs
his child ittn y a snak; or a missionary tlls you th dspair o th parnts at th loss o a child whom h had savd, a w yars or, rom ing immolatd at its irth. You larn that th “savag” mothrs usually nurs thir childrn till th ag o our, and that, in th Nw Hrids, on th loss o a spcially lovd child, its mothr, or aunt, will kill hrsl to tak car o it in th othr world.34 And so on.
     Lik acts ar mt with y th scor; so that, whn w s that ths
sam loving parnts practic inanticid, w ar ound to rcogniz that th hait (whatvr its ultrior transormations may ) took its origin undr th shr prssur o ncssity, as an oligation towards th tri, and a mans or raring th alrady growing childrn. Th savags, as a rul, do not “multiply without stint,” as som English writrs put it. On th contrary, thy tak all kinds o masurs or diminishing th irthrat. A whol sris o rstrictions, which Europans crtainly would nd travagant, ar imposd to that fct, and thy ar strictly oyd. But notwithstanding that, primitiv olk cannot rar all thir childrn. Howvr, it has n rmarkd that as soon as thy succd in incrasing thir rgular mans o susistnc, thy at onc gin to aandon th practic o inanticid. On th whol, th parnts oy that oligation rluctantly, and as soon as thy can aford it thy rsort to all kinds o compromiss to sav th livs o thir nw-orn. D R 
    M C
By pooling basic needs and medical aid in local distribution centers, people can provide health care and a base for searching for survivors, cleaning up, and rebuilding in the wake of disasters. Local distribution centers can often function as community meeting spaces, aiding in restoring a sense of agency and safety to local neighborhoods impacted by disaster.

##  B

The great migrations.—New organization rendered necessary.—The village community.—Communal work.—Judicial procedure—Inter-tribal law.— Illustrations from the life of our contemporaries—Buryates.—Kabyles.— Caucasian mountaineers.—African stems.
It is not possil to study primitiv mankind without ing dply imprssd y th sociaility it has displayd sinc its vry rst stps in li. Man is no cption in natur. H also is sujct to th grat principl o mutual aid which grants th st chancs o survival to thos who st support ach othr in th struggl or li. Ths wr th conclusions arrivd at in th prvious chaptrs.
      Howvr, as soon as w com to a highr stag o civilization, and
rr to history which alrady has somthing to say aout that stag, w ar wildrd y th struggls and conicts which it rvals. Th old onds sm ntirly to  rokn. Such was th social organization which dvlopd among th so-calld “ararians,” whn thy gan to sttl mor or lss prmanntly in Europ.
       A vry long volution was rquird or th gnts, or clans, rcognizd th sparat istnc o a patriarchal amily in a sparat hut; ut
vn ar that had n rcognizd, th clan, as a rul, knw no prsonal inhritanc o proprty. Th w things which might hav longd prsonally to th individual wr ithr dstroyd on his grav or urid with him. Th villag community, on th contrary, ully rcognizd th privat accumulation o walth within th amily and its hrditary transmission. But walth was concivd clusivly in th shap o movable proprty, including cattl, implmnts, arms, and th dwlling hous which—“lik all things that can  dstroyd y r”—longd to th sam catgory.6 As to privat proprty in land, th villag community did not, and could not, rcogniz anything o th kind, and, as a rul, it dos not rcogniz it now.
Th land was th common proprty o th tri, or o th whol stm, and th villag community itsl ownd its part o th trial trritory so long only as th tri did not claim a rdistriution o th villag allotmnts. Th claring o th woods and th raking o th prairis ing mostly don y th communitis or, at last, y th joint work o svral amilis—always with th consnt o th community—th clard plots wr hld y ach amily or a trm o our, twlv, or twnty yars, ar which trm thy wr tratd as parts o th aral land ownd in common. Privat proprty, or possssion “or vr” was as incompatil, with th vry principls and th rligious concptions o th villag community as it was with th principls o th gns; so that a long inunc o th Roman law and th Christian Church, which soon accptd th Roman principls, wr rquird to accustom th ararians to th ida o privat proprty in land ing possil.7 And yt, vn whn such proprty, or possssion or an unlimitd tim, was rcognizd, th ownr o a sparat stat rmaind a co-propritor in th wast lands, orsts, and grazing-grounds. Morovr, w continually s, spcially in th history o Russia, that whn a w amilis, acting sparatly, had takn possssion o som land longing to tris which wr tratd as strangrs, thy vry soon unitd togthr, and constitutd a villag community which in th third or ourth gnration gan to pross a community o origin.
     A whol sris o institutions, partly inhritd rom th clan priod,
hav dvlopd rom that asis o common ownrship o land during th long succssion o cnturis which was rquird to ring th ararians undr th dominion o Stats organizd upon th Roman or Byzantin pattrn. Th villag community was not only a union or guaranting to ach on his air shar in th common land, ut also a union or common cultur, or mutual support in all possil orms, or protction rom violnc, and or a urthr dvlopmnt o knowldg, national onds, and moral concptions; and vry chang in th judicial, military, ducational, or conomical mannrs had to  dcidd at th olkmots o th villag, th tri, or th condration. Th community ing a continuation o th gns, it inhritd all its unctions. It was th universitas, th mir—a world in itsl.
      Common hunting, common shing, and common cultur o th
orchards or th plantations o ruit trs was th rul with th old gnts. Common agricultur cam th rul in th ararian villag communitis. Tru, that dirct tstimony to this fct is scarc, and in th litratur o antiquity w only hav th passags o Diodorus and Julius Casar rlating to th inhaitants o th Lipari Islands, on o th Clt-Irian tris, and th Suvs. But thr is no lack o vidnc to prov that common

Morovr, it is wll known that many tris o Brazil, Cntral Amrica, and Mico usd to cultivat thir lds in common, and that th sam hait is widly sprad among som Malayans, in Nw Caldonia, with svral Ngro stms, and so on.11 In short, communal cultur is so haitual with many Aryan, Ural-Altayan, Mongolian, Ngro, Rd Indian, Malayan, and Mlansian stms that w must considr it as a univrsal—though not as th only possil—orm o primitiv agricultur.12
     Communal cultivation dos not, howvr, imply y ncssity communal consumption. Alrady undr th clan organization w on s
that whn th oats ladn with ruits or sh rturn to th villag, th ood thy ring in is dividd among th huts and th “long houss” inhaitd y ithr svral amilis or th youth, and is cookd sparatly at ach sparat harth. Th hait o taking mals in a narrowr circl o rlativs or associats thus prvails at an arly priod o clan li. It cam th rul in th villag community. Evn th ood grown in common was usually dividd twn th housholds ar part o it had n laid in stor or communal us. Howvr, th tradition o communal mals was piously kpt aliv; vry availal opportunity, such as th commmoration o th ancstors, th rligious stivals, th ginning and th nd o ld work, th irths, th marriags, and th unrals, ing sizd upon to ring th community to a common mal. Evn now this hait, wll known in this country as th “harvst suppr,” is th last to disappar. On th othr hand, vn whn th lds had long sinc casd to  tilld and sown in common, a varity o agricultural work continud, and continus still, to  prormd y th community. Som part o th communal land is still cultivatd in many cass in common, ithr or th us o th dstitut, or or rlling th communal stors, or or using th produc at th rligious stivals. Th irrigation canals ar diggd and rpaird in common. Th communal madows ar mown y th community; and th sight o a Russian commun mowing a madow—th mn rivalling ach othr in thir advanc with th scyth, whil th womn turn th grass ovr and throw it up into haps—is on o th most inspiring sights; it shows what human
work might  and ought to . Th hay, in such cas, is dividd among th sparat housholds, and it is vidnt that no on has th right o taking hay rom a nighour’s stack without his prmission; ut th limitation o this last rul among th Caucasian Ossts is most notworthy. Whn th cuckoo cris and announcs that spring is coming, and that th madows will soon  clothd again with grass, vry on in nd has th right o taking rom a nighour’s stack th hay h wants or his cattl.13 Th old communal rights ar thus r-assrtd, as i to prov how contrary unridld individualism is to human natur.
      Whn th Europan travllr lands in som small island o th Pacic,
and, sing at a distanc a grov o palm trs, walks in that dirction, h is astonishd to discovr that th littl villags ar connctd y roads pavd with ig stons, quit comortal or th unshod nativs, and vry similar to th “old roads” o th Swiss mountains. Such roads wr tracd y th “ararians” all ovr Europ, and on must hav travlld in wild, thinly popld countris, ar away rom th chi lins o communication, to raliz in ull th immns work that must hav n prormd y th ararian communitis in ordr to conqur th woody and marshy wildrnss which Europ was som two thousand yars ago. Isolatd amilis, having no tools, and wak as thy wr, could not hav conqurd it; th wildrnss would hav ovrpowrd thm. Villag communitis alon, working in common, could mastr th wild orsts, th sinking marshs, and th ndlss stpps. Th rough roads, th rris, th woodn ridgs takn away in th wintr and ruilt ar th spring ood was ovr, th ncs and th palisadd walls o th villags, th arthn orts and th small towrs with which th trritory was dottd—all ths wr th work o th ararian communitis. And whn a community grw numrous it usd to throw of a nw ud. A nw community aros at a distanc, thus stp y stp ringing th woods and th stpps undr th dominion o man. Th whol making o Europan nations was such a udding o th villag communitis. Evn now-a-days th Russian pasants, i thy ar not quit rokn down y misry, migrat in communitis, and thy till th soil and uild th houss in common whn thy sttl on th anks o th Amur, or in Manitoa. And vn th English, whn thy rst gan to coloniz Amrica, usd to rturn to th old systm; thy groupd into villag communitis.14
      Th villag community was th chi arm o th ararians in thir
hard struggl against a hostil natur. It also was th ond thy opposd to opprssion y th cunningst and th strongst which so asily might hav dvlopd during thos disturd tims. Th imaginary ararian—th
man who ghts and kills at his mr capric—istd no mor than th “loodthirsty” savag. Th ral ararian was living, on th contrary, undr a wid sris o institutions, imud with considrations as to what may  usul or noious to his tri or condration, and ths institutions wr piously handd down rom gnration to gnration in vrss and songs, in provrs or triads, in sntncs and instructions. Th mor w study thm th mor w rcogniz th narrow onds which unitd mn in thir villags. Evry quarrl arising twn two individuals was tratd as a communal afair—vn th ofnsiv words that might hav n uttrd during a quarrl ing considrd as an ofnc to th community and its ancstors. Thy had to  rpaird y amnds mad oth to th individual and th community;15 and i a quarrl ndd in a ght and wounds, th man who stood y and did not intrpos was tratd as i h himsl had inictd th wounds.16 Th judicial procdur was imud with th sam spirit. Evry disput was rought rst or mdiators or aritrs, and it mostly ndd with thm, th aritrs playing a vry important part in ararian socity. But i th cas was too grav to  sttld in this way, it cam or th olkmot, which was ound “to nd th sntnc,” and pronouncd it in a conditional orm; that is, “such compnsation was du, i th wrong  provd,” and th wrong had to  provd or disclaimd y si or twlv prsons conrming or dnying th act y oath; ordal ing rsortd to in cas o contradiction twn th two sts o jurors. Such procdur, which rmaind in orc or mor than two thousand yars in succssion, spaks volums or itsl; it shows how clos wr th onds twn all mmrs o th community. Morovr, thr was no othr authority to norc th dcisions o th olkmot sids its own moral authority. Th only possil mnac was that th community might dclar th rl an outlaw, ut vn this mnac was rciprocal. A man discontntd with th olkmot could dclar that h would aandon th tri and go ovr to anothr tri—a most dradul mnac, as it was sur to ring all kinds o misortuns upon a tri that might hav n unair to on o its mmrs.17 A rllion against a right dcision o th customary law was simply “inconcival,” as Hnry Main has so wll said, caus “law, morality, and act” could not  sparatd rom ach othr in thos tims.18 Th moral authority o th commun was so grat that vn at a much latr poch, whn th villag communitis ll into sumission to th udal lord, thy maintaind thir judicial powrs; thy only prmittd th lord, or his dputy, to “nd” th aov conditional sntnc in accordanc with th customary law h had sworn to ollow, and to lvy or himsl th n (th fred) du to th commun. But or a long tim, th lord himsl, i
h rmaind a co-propritor in th wast land o th commun, sumittd in communal afairs to its dcisions. Nol or cclsiastic, h had to sumit to th olkmot—Wer daselbst Wasser und Weid genusst, muss gehorsam sein— “Who njoys hr th right o watr and pastur must oy”—was th old saying. Evn whn th pasants cam srs undr th lord, h was ound to appar or th olkmot whn thy summond him.19
       In thir concptions o justic th ararians vidntly did not much
difr rom th savags. Thy also maintaind th ida that a murdr must  ollowd y putting th murdrr to dath; that wounds had to  punishd y qual wounds, and that th wrongd amily was ound to ull th sntnc o th customary law. This was a holy duty, a duty towards th ancstors, which had to  accomplishd in road daylight, nvr in scrcy, and rndrd widly known. Thror th most inspird passags o th sagas and pic potry altogthr ar thos which gloriy what was supposd to  justic. Th gods thmslvs joind in aiding it. Howvr, th prdominant atur o ararian justic is, on th on hand, to limit th numrs o prsons who may  involvd in a ud, and, on th othr hand, to tirpat th rutal ida o lood or lood and wounds or wounds, y sustituting or it th systm o compnsation. Th ararian cods which wr collctions o common law ruls writtn down or th us o judgs—“rst prmittd, thn ncouragd, and at last norcd,” compnsation instad o rvng.20 Th compnsation has, howvr, n totally misundrstood y thos who rprsntd it as a n, and as a sort o carte blanche givn to th rich man to do whatvr h likd. Th compnsation mony (wergeld), which was quit difrnt rom th n or fred,21 was haitually so high or all kinds o activ ofncs that it crtainly was no ncouragmnt or such ofncs. In cas o a murdr it usually cdd all th possil ortun o th murdrr “Eightn tims ightn cows” is th compnsation with th Ossts who do not know how to rckon aov ightn, whil with th Arican tris it attains  cows or  camls with thir young, or  shp in th poorr tris.22 In th grat majority o cass, th compnsation mony could not  paid at all, so that th murdrr had no issu ut to induc th wrongd amily, y rpntanc, to adopt him. Evn now, in th Caucasus, whn uds com to an nd, th ofndr touchs with his lips th rast o th oldst woman o th tri, and coms a “milk-rothr” to all mn o th wrongd amily.23 With svral Arican tris h must giv his daughtr, or sistr, in marriag to som on o th amily; with othr tris h is ound to marry th woman whom h has mad a widow; and in all cass h coms a mmr o th amily, whos opinion is takn in all important amily mattrs.24
     Far rom acting with disrgard to human li, th ararians, mor-
ovr, knw nothing o th horrid punishmnts introducd at a latr poch y th laic and canonic laws undr Roman and Byzantin inunc. For, i th Saon cod admittd th dath pnalty rathr rly vn in cass o incndiarism and armd rory, th othr ararian cods pronouncd it clusivly in cass o trayal o on’s kin, and sacrilg against th community’s gods, as th only mans to appas th gods.
     All this, as sn is vry ar rom th supposd “moral dissolutnss”
o th ararians. On th contrary, w cannot ut admir th dply moral principls laoratd within th arly villag communitis which ound thir prssion in Wlsh triads, in lgnds aout King Arthur, in Brhon commntaris,25 in old Grman lgnds and so on, or nd still thir prssion in th sayings o th modrn ararians. In his introduction to The Story of Burnt Njal, Gorg Dasnt vry justly sums up as ollows th qualitis o a Northman, as thy appar in th sagas:
    To do what lay or him opnly and lik a man, without ar o
    ithr os, nds, or at; . . . to  r and daring in all his dds;
    to  gntl and gnrous to his rinds and kinsmn; to  strn
    and grim to his os [thos who ar undr th lex talionis], ut vn
    towards thm to ull all oundn dutis. . . . To  no truc-rakr,
    nor tal-arr, nor ackitr. To uttr nothing against any man that
    h would not dar to tll him to his ac. To turn no man rom his door
    who sought ood or shltr, vn though h wr a o.26
Th sam or still ttr principls prmat th Wlsh pic potry and triads. To act “according to th natur o mildnss and th principls o quity,” without rgard to th os or to th rinds, and “to rpair th wrong,” ar th highst dutis o man; “vil is dath, good is li,” claims th pot lgislator.27 “Th World would  ool, i agrmnts mad on lips wr not honoural”—th Brhon law says. And th huml Shamanist Mordovian, ar having praisd th sam qualitis, will add, morovr, in his principls o customary law, that “among nighours th cow and th milking-jar ar in common.” that, “th cow must  milkd or yoursl and him who may ask milk”; that “th ody o a child rddns rom th strok, ut th ac o him who striks rddns rom sham”; and so on.28 Many pags might  lld with lik principls prssd and ollowd y th “ararians.”
     On atur mor o th old villag communitis dsrvs a spcial
mntion. It is th gradual tnsion o th circl o mn mracd y th lings o solidarity. Not only th tris dratd into stms, ut th
stms as wll, vn though o difrnt origin, joind togthr in cond- rations. Som unions wr so clos that, or instanc, th Vandals, ar part o thir condration had l or th Rhin, and thnc wnt ovr to Spain and Arica, rspctd or orty conscutiv yars th landmarks and th aandond villags o thir condrats, and did not tak possssion o thm until thy had ascrtaind through nvoys that thir condrats did not intnd to rturn. With othr ararians, th soil was cultivatd y on part o th stm, whil th othr part ought on or yond th rontirs o th common trritory. As to th lagus twn svral stms, thy wr quit haitual. Th Sicamrs unitd with th Chrusqus and th Suvs, th Quads with th Sarmats; th Sarmats with th Alans, th Carps, and th Huns. Latr on, w also s th concption o nations gradually dvloping in Europ, long or anything lik a Stat had grown in any part o th continnt occupid y th ararians. Ths nations—or it is impossil to rus th nam o a nation to th Mrovingian Franc, or to th Russia o th lvnth and twlh cntury—wr nvrthlss kpt togthr y nothing ls ut a community o languag, and a tacit agr- mnt o th small rpulics to tak thir duks rom non ut on spcial amily.
      Wars wr crtainly unavoidal; migration mans war; ut Sir Hnry
Main has alrady ully provd in his rmarkal study o th trial origin o Intrnational Law, that “Man has nvr n so rocious or so stupid as to sumit to such an vil as war without som kind o fort to prvnt it,” and h has shown how cdingly grat is “th numr o ancint institutions which ar th marks o a dsign to stand in th way o war, or to provid an altrnativ to it.”29 In rality, man is so ar rom th warlik ing h is supposd to , that whn th ararians had onc sttld thy so rapidly lost th vry haits o warar that vry soon thy wr complld to kp spcial duks ollowd y spcial scholae or ands o warriors, in ordr to protct thm rom possil intrudrs. Thy prrrd pacul toil to war, th vry paculnss o man ing th caus o th spcialization o th warrior’s trad, which spcialization rsultd latr on in srdom and in all th wars o th “Stats priod” o human history.
      History nds grat dicultis in rstoring to li th institutions o th
ararians. At vry stp th historian mts with som aint indication which h is unal to plain with th aid o his own documnts only. But a road light is thrown on th past as soon as w rr to th institutions o th vry numrous tris which ar still living undr a social organization almost idntical with that o our ararian ancstors. Hr w simply hav th diculty o choic, caus th islands o th Pacic, th stpps
o Asia, and th tallands o Arica ar ral historical musums containing spcimns o all possil intrmdiat stags which mankind has livd through, whn passing rom th savag gnts up to th Stats’ organization. Lt us, thn, amin a w o thos spcimns.
      I w tak th villag communitis o th Mongol Buryats, spcially
thos o th Kudinsk Stpp on th uppr Lna which hav ttr scapd Russian inunc, w hav air rprsntativs o ararians in a transitional stat, twn cattl-rding and agricultur.30 Ths Buryats ar still living in “joint amilis”; that is, although ach son, whn h is marrid, gos to liv in a sparat hut, th huts o at last thr gnrations rmain within th sam nclosur, and th joint amily work in common in thir lds, and own in common thir joint housholds and thir cattl, as wll as thir “calvs’ grounds” (small ncd patchs o soil kpt undr so grass or th raring o calvs). As a rul, th mals ar takn sparatly in ach hut; ut whn mat is roastd, all th twnty to sity mmrs o th joint houshold ast togthr. Svral joint housholds which liv in a clustr, as wll as svral smallr amilis sttld in th sam villag—mostly débris o joint housholds accidntally rokn up—mak th oulous, or th villag community; svral oulouses mak a tri; and th orty-si tris, or clans, o th Kudinsk Stpp ar unitd into on condration. Smallr and closr condrations ar ntrd into, as ncssity ariss or spcial wants, y svral tris. Thy know no privat proprty in land—th land ing hld in common y th oulous, or rathr y th condration, and i it coms ncssary, th trritory is r-allottd twn th difrnt oulouses at a olkmot o th tri, and twn th orty-si tris at a olkmot o th condration. It is worthy o not that th sam organization prvails among all th , Buryats o East Siria, although thy hav n or thr cnturis undr Russian rul, and ar wll acquaintd with Russian institutions.
      With all that, inqualitis o ortun rapidly dvlop among th
Buryats, spcially sinc th Russian Govrnmnt is giving an aggratd importanc to thir lctd taishas (princs), whom it considrs as rsponsil ta-collctors and rprsntativs o th condrations in thir administrativ and vn commrcial rlations with th Russians. Th channls or th nrichmnt o th w ar thus many, whil th impovrishmnt o th grat numr gos hand in hand, through th appropriation o th Buryat lands y th Russians. But it is a hait with th Buryats, sp- cially thos o Kudinsk—and hait is mor than law—that i a amily has lost its cattl, th richr amilis giv it som cows and horss that it may rcovr. As to th dstitut man who has no amily, h taks his mals in th
huts o his congnrs; h ntrs a hut, taks—y right, not or charity—his sat y th r, and shars th mal which always is scrupulously dividd into qual parts; h slps whr h has takn his vning mal. Altogthr, th Russian conqurors o Siria wr so much struck y th communistic practics o th Buryats, that thy gav thm th nam o Bratskiye—“th Brothrly Ons”—and rportd to Moscow. “With thm vrything is in common; whatvr thy hav is shard in common.” Evn now, whn th Lna Buryats sll thir what, or snd som o thir cattl to  sold to a Russian utchr, th amilis o th oulous, or th tri, put thir what and cattl togthr, and sll it as a whol. Each oulous has, morovr, its grain stor or loans in cas o nd, its communal aking ovn (th four banal o th old Frnch communitis), and its lacksmith, who, lik th lacksmith o th Indian communitis,31 ing a mmr o th community, is nvr paid or his work within th community. H must mak it or nothing, and i h utilizs his spar tim or aricating th small plats o chislld and silvrd iron which ar usd in Buryat land or th dcoration o drss, h may occasionally sll thm to a woman rom anothr clan, ut to th womn o his own clan th attir is prsntd as a gi. Slling and uying cannot tak plac within th community, and th rul is so svr that whn a richr amily hirs a laourr th laourr must  takn rom anothr clan or rom among th Russians. This hait is vidntly not spcic to th Buryats; it is so widly sprad among th modrn ararians, Aryan and Ural-Altayan, that it must hav n univrsal among our ancstors.
     Th ling o union within th condration is kpt aliv y th
common intrsts o th tris, thir olkmots, and th stivitis which ar usually kpt in connction with th olkmots. Th sam ling is, howvr, maintaind y anothr institution, th aba, or common hunt, which is a rminiscnc o a vry rmot past. Evry autumn, th orty-si clans o Kudinsk com togthr or such a hunt, th produc o which is dividd among all th amilis. Morovr, national abas, to assrt th unity o th whol Buryat nation, ar convokd rom tim to tim. In such cass, all Buryat clans which ar scattrd or hundrds o mils wst and ast o Lak Baikal, ar ound to snd thir dlgat huntrs. Thousands o mn com togthr, ach on ringing provisions or a whol month. Evry on’s shar must  qual to all th othrs, and thror, or ing put togthr, thy ar wighd y an lctd ldr (always “with th hand”: scals would  a proanation o th old custom). Ar that th huntrs divid into ands o twnty, and th partis go hunting according to a wll-sttld plan. In such abas th ntir Buryat nation rvivs its pic traditions o a tim whn it was unitd in a powrul lagu. Lt m add
that such communal hunts ar quit usual with th Rd Indians and th Chins on th anks o th Usuri (the kada).32
      With th Kayls, whos mannrs o li hav n so wll dscrid
y two Frnch plorrs,33 w hav ararians still mor advancd in agricultur. Thir lds, irrigatd and manurd, ar wll attndd to, and in th hilly tracts vry availal plot o land is cultivatd y th spad. Th Kayls hav known many vicissituds in thir history; thy hav ollowd or som tim th Mussulman law o inhritanc, ut, ing advrs to it, thy hav rturnd,  yars ago, to th trial customary law o old. Accordingly, thir land-tnur is o a mid charactr, and privat proprty in land ists sid y sid with communal possssion. Still, th asis o thir prsnt organization is th villag community, th thaddart, which usually consists o svral joint amilis (kharoubas), claiming a community o origin, as wll as o smallr amilis o strangrs. Svral villags ar groupd into clans or tris (ârch); svral tris mak th condration (thak’ebilt); and svral condrations may occasionally ntr into a lagu, chiy or purposs o armd dnc.
      Th Kayls know no authority whatvr sids that o th djemmâa,
or olkmot o th villag community. All mn o ag tak part in it, in th opn air, or in a spcial uilding providd with ston sats, and th dcisions o th djemmâa ar vidntly takn at unanimity: that is, th discussions continu until all prsnt agr to accpt, or to sumit to, som dcision. Thr ing no authority in a villag community to impos a dcision, this systm has n practicd y mankind whrvr thr hav n villag communitis, and it is practicd still whrvr thy continu to ist, i.. y svral hundrd million mn all ovr th world. Th djemmâa nominats its cutiv—th ldr, th scri, and th trasurr; it asssss its own tas; and it manags th rpartition o th common lands, as wll as all kinds o works o pulic utility. A grat dal o work is don in common: th roads, th mosqus, th ountains, th irrigation canals, th towrs rctd or protction rom rors, th ncs, and so on, ar uilt y th villag community; whil th high-roads, th largr mosqus, and th grat markt-placs ar th work o th tri. Many tracs o common cultur continu to ist, and th houss continu to  uilt y, or with th aid o, all mn and womn o th villag. Altogthr, th “aids” ar o daily occurrnc, and ar continually calld in or th cultivation o th lds, or harvsting, and so on. As to th skilld work, ach community has its lacksmith, who njoys his part o th communal land, and works or th community; whn th tilling sason approachs h visits vry hous, and rpairs th tools and th ploughs, without pcting any pay, whil th
making o nw ploughs is considrd as a pious work which can y no mans  rcompnsd in mony, or y any othr orm o salary.
     As th Kayls alrady hav privat proprty, thy vidntly hav oth
rich and poor among thm. But lik all popl who closly liv togthr, and know how povrty gins, thy considr it as an accidnt which may visit vry on. “Don’t say that you will nvr war th ggar’s ag, nor go to prison,” is a provr o th Russian pasants; th Kayls practic it, and no difrnc can  dtctd in th trnal haviour twn rich and poor; whn th poor convoks an “aid,” th rich man works in his ld, just as th poor man dos it rciprocally in his turn.34 Morovr, th djemmâas st asid crtain gardns and lds, somtims cultivatd in common, or th us o th poorst mmrs. Many lik customs continu to ist. As th poorr amilis would not  al to uy mat, mat is rgularly ought with th mony o th ns, or th gis to th djemmâa, or th paymnts or th us o th communal oliv-oil asins, and it is distriutd in qual parts among thos who cannot aford uying mat thmslvs. And whn a shp or a ullock is killd y a amily or its own us on a day which is not a markt day, th act is announcd in th strts y th villag crir, in ordr that sick popl and prgnant womn may tak o it what thy want. Mutual support prmats th li o th Kayls, and i on o thm, during a journy aroad, mts with anothr Kayl in nd, h is ound to com to his aid, vn at th risk o his own ortun and li; i this has not n don, th djemmâa o th man who has sufrd rom such nglct may lodg a complaint, and th djemmâa o th slsh man will at onc mak good th loss. W thus com across a custom which is amiliar to th studnts o th mdival mrchant guilds. Evry strangr who ntrs a Kayl villag has right to housing in th wintr, and his horss can always graz on th communal lands or twnty-our hours. But in cas o nd h can rckon upon an almost unlimitd support. Thus, during th amin o –, th Kayls rcivd and d vry on who sought rug in thir villags, without distinction o origin. In th district o Dllys, no lss than , popl who cam rom all parts o Algria, and vn rom Morocco, wr d in this way. Whil popl did rom starvation all ovr Algria, thr was not on singl cas o dath du to this caus on Kaylian soil. Th djemmâas, dpriving thmslvs o ncssaris, organizd rli, without vr asking any aid rom th Govrnmnt, or uttring th slightst complaint; thy considrd it as a natural duty. And whil among th Europan sttlrs all kind o polic masurs wr takn to prvnt ths and disordr rsulting rom such an inu o strangrs, nothing o th kind was rquird on th Kayls’ trritory: th djemmâas ndd nithr aid nor protction rom without.35
       I can only cursorily mntion two othr most intrsting aturs
o Kayl li; namly, th anaya, or protction grantd to wlls, canals, mosqus, marktplacs, som roads, and so on, in cas o war, and th çofs. In th anaya w hav a sris o institutions oth or diminishing th vils o war and or prvnting conicts. Thus th markt-plac is anaya, spcially i it stands on a rontir and rings Kayls and strangrs togthr; no on dars distur pac in th markt, and i a disturanc ariss, it is qulld at onc y th strangrs who hav gathrd in th markt town. Th road upon which th womn go rom th villag to th ountain also is anaya in cas o war; and so on. As to th çof it is a widly sprad orm o association, having som charactrs o th mdival Bürgschaen or Gegilden, as wll as o socitis oth or mutual protction and or various purposs— intllctual, political, and motional—which cannot  satisd y th trritorial organization o th villag, th clan, and th con dration. Th çof knows no trritorial limits; it rcruits its mmrs in various villags, vn among strangrs; and it protcts thm in all possil vntualitis o li. Altogthr, it is an attmpt at supplmnting th trritorial grouping y an tra-trritorial grouping intndd to giv an prssion to mutual anitis o all kinds across th rontirs. Th r intrnational association o individual tasts and idas, which w considr as on o th st aturs o our own li, has thus its origin in ararian antiquity.
       Th mountainrs o Caucasia ofr anothr trmly instructiv
ld or illustrations o th sam kind. than twnty Gorgian and Tartar villags. Th had-drss o th womn is anaya. I a quarrl has not n stoppd in tim and has ndd in murdr, th compnsation mony is so considral that th aggrssor is ntirly ruind or his li, unlss h is adoptd y th wrongd amily; and i h has rsortd to his sword in a triing quarrl and has inictd wounds, h loss or vr th considration o his kin. In all disputs, mdiators tak th mattr in hand; thy slct rom among th mmrs o th clan th judgs—si in smallr afairs, and rom tn to n in mor srious mattrs—and Russian osrvrs tstiy to th asolut incorruptiility o th judgs.      Th stms o Arica ofr such an immns varity o trmly intr-
sting socitis standing at all intrmdiat stags rom th arly villag community to th dspotic ararian monarchis that I must aandon th ida o giving hr vn th chi rsults o a comparativ study o thir
institutions.38 Suc it to say, that, vn undr th most horrid dspotism o kings, th olkmots o th villag communitis and thir customary law rmain sovrign in a wid circl o afairs.      Th villag communitis o th nativs o oth Amricas hav th sam
charactr. Th Tupi o Brazil wr ound living in “long houss” occupid y whol clans which usd to cultivat thir corn and manioc lds in common. At anothr trmity o th world w nd th Malayan udalism, ut this udalism has n powrlss to unroot th negaria, or villag community, with its common ownrship o at last part o th land, and th rdistriution o land among th svral negarias o th tri.40 With th Alurus o Minahasa w nd th communal rotation o th crops; with th Indian stm o th Wyandots w hav th priodical rdistriution o land within th tri, and th clan-cultur o th soil; and in all thos parts o Sumatra whr Moslm institutions hav not yt totally dstroyd th old organization w nd th joint amily (suka) and th villag community (kota) which maintains its right upon th land, vn i part o it has n clard without its authorization.41 But to say this, is to say that all customs or mutual protction and prvntion o uds and wars, which hav n riy indicatd in th prcding pags as charactristic o th villag community, ist as wll. Mor than that: th mor ully th communal possssion o land has n maintaind, th ttr and th gntlr ar th haits. D Sturs positivly arms that whrvr th institution o th villag community has n lss ncroachd upon y th conqurors, th inqualitis o ortuns ar smallr, and th vry prscriptions o th lex talionis ar lss crul; whil, on th contrary, whrvr th villag community has n totally rokn up, “th inhaitants sufr th most unaral opprssion rom thir dspotic rulrs.”42 This is quit natural.
And whn Waitz mad th rmark that thos stms which hav maintaind thir trial condrations stand on a highr lvl o dvlopmnt and hav a richr litratur than thos stms which hav oritd th old onds o union, h only pointd out what might hav n ortold in advanc.
      Mor illustrations would simply involv m in tdious rptitions—so
strikingly similar ar th ararian socitis undr all climats and amidst all racs. Th sam procss o volution has n going on in mankind with a wondrul similarity. Whn th clan organization, assaild as it was rom within y th sparat amily, and rom without y th dismmrmnt o th migrating clans and th ncssity o taking in strangrs o difr- nt dscnt—th villag community, asd upon a trritorial concption, cam into istnc. This nw institution, which had naturally grown out o th prcding on—th clan—prmittd th ararians to pass through a most disturd priod o history without ing rokn into isolatd amilis which would hav succumd in th struggl or li. Nw orms o cultur dvlopd undr th nw organization; agricultur attaind th stag which it hardly has surpassd until now with th grat numr; th domstic industris rachd a high dgr o prction. Th wildrnss was conqurd, it was intrsctd y roads, dottd with swarms thrown of y th mothr-communitis. Markts and ortid cntrs, as wll as placs o pulic worship, wr rctd. Th concptions o a widr union, tndd to whol stms and to svral stms o various origin, wr slowly laoratd. Th old concptions o justic which wr concptions o mr rvng, slowly undrwnt a dp modication—th ida o amnds or th wrong don taking th plac o rvng. Th customary law which still maks th law o th daily li or two-thirds or mor o mankind, was laoratd undr that organization, as wll as a systm o haits intndd to prvnt th opprssion o th masss y th minoritis whos powrs grw in proportion to th growing acilitis or privat accumulation o walth. This was th nw orm takn y th tndncis o th masss or mutual support. And th progrss—conomical, intllctual, and moral— which mankind accomplishd undr this nw popular orm o organization, was so grat that th Stats, whn thy wr calld latr on into istnc, simply took possssion, in th intrst o th minoritis, o all th judicial, conomical, and administrativ unctions which th villag community alrady had rcisd in th intrst o all.
          B S
Aid to people seeking to cross borders disrupts the violence and harm caused by borders. People lay out caches of lifesaving water, food, and medical supplies for people crossing deserts, while others may use ships to support individuals crossing seas.
