M A  
## M C

Growth of authority in Barbarian Society.—Serfdom in the villages.—Revolt of fortied towns: their liberation; their charts.—The guild.—Double origin of the free medieval city.—Self-jurisdiction, self-administration.—Honourable position of labour.—Trade by the guild and by the city.
Sociaility and nd o mutual aid and support ar such inhrnt parts o human natur that at no tim o history can w discovr mn living in small isolatd amilis, ghting ach othr or th mans o susistnc. On th contrary, modrn rsarch, as w saw it in th two prcding chaptrs, provs that sinc th vry ginning o thir prhistoric li mn usd to agglomrat into gnts, clans, or tris, maintaind y an ida o common dscnt and y worship o common ancstors. For thousands and thousands o yars this organization has kpt mn togthr, vn though thr was no authority whatvr to impos it. It has dply imprssd all sus- qunt dvlopmnt o mankind; and whn th onds o common dscnt had n loosnd y migrations on a grand scal, whil th dvlopmnt o th sparatd amily within th clan itsl had dstroyd th old unity o th clan, a nw orm o union, trritorial in its principl—th villag community—was calld into istnc y th social gnius o man. This institution, again, kpt mn togthr or a numr o cnturis, prmitting thm to urthr dvlop thir social institutions and to pass through som o th darkst priods o history, without ing dissolvd into loos aggr- gations o amilis and individuals, to mak a urthr stp in thir volution, and to work out a numr o scondary social institutions, svral o which hav survivd down to th prsnt tim. W hav now to ollow th urthr dvlopmnts o th sam vr-living tndncy or mutual aid. Taking th villag communitis o th so-calld ararians at a tim whn thy wr making a nw start o civilization ar th all o th Roman Empir, w hav to study th nw aspcts takn y th social wants o th masss in th middl ags, and spcially in th mdival guilds and th mdival city.
     Far rom ing th ghting animals thy hav on n compard to,
th ararians o th rst cnturis o our ra (lik so many Mongolians, Aricans, Aras, and so on, who still continu in th sam ararian stag) invarialy prrrd pac to war. With th cption o a w tris which had n drivn during th grat migrations into unproductiv dsrts or
highlands, and wr thus complld priodically to pry upon thir ttr- avourd nighours—apart rom ths, th grat ulk o th Tutons, th Saons, th Clts, th Slavonians, and so on, vry soon ar thy had sttld in thir nwly conqurd aods, rvrtd to th spad or to thir hrds. Th arlist ararian cods alrady rprsnt to us socitis composd o pacul agricultural communitis, not hords o mn at war with ach othr. Ths ararians covrd th country with villags and armhouss;1 thy clard th orsts, ridgd th torrnts, and colonizd th ormrly quit uninhaitd wildrnss; and thy l th uncrtain warlik pursuits to rothrhoods, scholae, or “trusts” o unruly mn, gathrd round tmporary chiains, who wandrd aout, ofring thir advnturous spirit, thir arms, and thir knowldg o warar or th protction o populations, only too anious to  l in pac. Th warrior ands cam and wnt, proscuting thir amily uds; ut th grat mass continud to till th soil, taking ut littl notic o thir would- rulrs, so long as thy did not intrr with th indpndnc o thir villag communitis.2 Th nw occupirs o Europ volvd th systms o land tnur and soil cultur which ar still in orc with hundrds o millions o mn; thy workd out thir systms o compnsation or wrongs, instad o th old trial lood rvng; thy larnd th rst rudimnts o industry; and whil thy orti- d thir villags with palisadd walls, or rctd towrs and arthn orts whrto to rpair in cas o a nw invasion, thy soon aandond th task o dnding ths towrs and orts to thos who mad o war a spciality.
      Th vry paculnss o th ararians, crtainly not thir supposd
warlik instincts, thus cam th sourc o thir susqunt sujction to th military chiains. It is vidnt that th vry mod o li o th armd rothrhoods ofrd thm mor acilitis or nrichmnt than th tillrs o th soil could nd in thir agricultural communitis. Evn now w s that armd mn occasionally com togthr to shoot down Matals and to ro thm o thir drovs o cattl, though th Matals only want pac and ar rady to uy it at a high pric. Th scholae o old crtainly wr not mor scrupulous than th scholae o our own tim. Drovs o cattl, iron (which was trmly costly at that tim),3 and slavs wr appropriatd in this way; and although most acquisitions wr wastd on th spot in thos glorious asts o which pic potry has so much to say—still som part o th rod richs was usd or urthr nrichmnt. Thr was plnty o wast land, and no lack o mn rady to till it, i only thy could otain th ncssary cattl and implmnts. Whol villags, ruind y murrains, psts, rs, or raids o nw immigrants, wr on aandond y thir inhaitants, who wnt anywhr in sarch o nw aods. Thy still do so
in Russia in similar circumstancs. And i on o th hirdmen o th armd rothrhoods ofrd th pasants som cattl or a rsh start, som iron to mak a plough, i not th plough itsl, his protction rom urthr raids, and a numr o yars r rom all oligations, or thy should gin to rpay th contractd dt, thy sttld upon th land. And whn, ar a hard ght with ad crops, inundations and pstilncs, thos pionrs gan to rpay thir dts, thy ll into srvil oligations towards th protctor o th trritory. Walth undoutdly did accumulat in this way, and powr always ollows walth.4 And yt, th mor w pntrat into th li o thos tims, th sith and svnth cnturis o our ra, th mor w s that anothr lmnt, sids walth and military orc, was rquird to constitut th authority o th w. It was an lmnt o law and right, a dsir o th masss to maintain pac, and to stalish what thy consid- rd to  justic, which gav to th chiains o th scholae—kings, duks, knyazs, and th lik—th orc thy acquird two or thr hundrd yars latr. That sam ida o justic, concivd as an adquat rvng or th wrong don, which had grown in th trial stag, now passd as a rd thrad through th history o susqunt institutions, and, much mor vn than military or conomic causs, it cam th asis upon which th authority o th kings and th udal lords was oundd.
      In act, on o th chi proccupations o th ararian villag community always was, as it still is with our ararian contmporaris, to put
a spdy nd to th uds which aros rom th thn currnt concption o justic. Whn a quarrl took plac, th community at onc intrrd, and ar th olkmot had hard th cas, it sttld th amount o composition (wergeld) to  paid to th wrongd prson, or to his amily, as wll as th fred, or n or rach o pac, which had to  paid to th community. Intrior quarrls wr asily appasd in this way. But whn uds rok out twn two difrnt tris, or two condrations o tris, notwithstanding all masurs takn to prvnt thm,5 th diculty was to nd an aritr or sntnc-ndr whos dcision should  accptd y oth partis alik, oth or his impartiality and or his knowldg o th oldst law. Th diculty was th gratr as th customary laws o difrnt tris and condrations wr at varianc as to th compnsation du in difrnt cass. It thror cam haitual to tak th sntnc-ndr rom among such amilis, or such tris, as wr rputd or kping th law o old in its purity; o ing vrsd in th songs, triads, sagas, tc., y mans o which law was prptuatd in mmory; and to rtain law in this way cam a sort o art, a “mystry,” carully transmittd in crtain amilis rom gnration to gnration. Thus in Icland, and in othr Scandinavian lands, at vry
Allthing, or national olkmot, a lövsögmathr usd to rcit th whol law rom mmory or th nlightning o th assmly; and in Irland thr was, as is known, a spcial class o mn rputd or th knowldg o th old traditions, and thror njoying a grat authority as judgs.6 Again, whn w ar told y th Russian annals that som stms o North-Wst Russia, movd y th growing disordr which rsultd rom “clans rising against clans,” appald to Norman varingiar to  thir judgs and commandrs o warrior scholae; and whn w s th knyazes, or duks, lctd or th nt two hundrd yars always rom th sam Norman amily, w cannot ut rcogniz that th Slavonians trustd to th Normans or a ttr knowldg o th law which would  qually rcognizd as good y difrnt Slavonian kins. In this cas th possssion o runs, usd or th transmission o old customs, was a dcidd advantag in avour o th Normans; ut in othr cass thr ar aint indications that th “ldst” ranch o th stm, th supposd mothrranch, was appald to to supply th judgs, and its dcisions wr rlid upon as just;7 whil at a latr poch w s a distinct tndncy towards taking th sntnc-ndrs rom th Christian clrgy, which, at that tim, kpt still to th undamntal, now orgottn, principl o Christianity, that rtaliation is no act o justic. At that tim th Christian clrgy opnd th churchs as placs o asylum or thos who d rom lood rvng, and thy willingly actd as aritrs in criminal cass, always opposing th old trial principl o li or li and wound or wound. In short, th dpr w pntrat into th history o arly institutions, th lss w nd grounds or th military thory o origin o authority. In Italy th young communs wr continually snding away thir defensors or domini, ghting thos who rusd to go. Th sam wnt on in th East. In Bohmia, rich and poor alik (Bohemicae gentis magni et parvi, nobiles et ignobiles) took part in th lction;15 whil, th vyeches (olkmots) o th Russian citis rgularly lctd thir duks—always rom th sam Rurik amily—covnantd with thm, and snt th knyaz away i h had provokd discontnt.16 At th sam tim in most citis o Wstrn and Southrn Europ, th tndncy was to tak or defensor a ishop whom th city had lctd itsl. and so many ishops took th lad in protcting th “immunitis” o th towns and in dnding thir lirtis, that numrs o thm wr considrd, ar thir dath, as saints and spcial patrons o difrnt citis. St. Uthlrd o Winchstr, St. Ulrik o Augsurg, St. Wolgang o Ratison, St. Hrirt o Cologn, St. Adalrt o Pragu, and so on, as wll as many aots and monks, cam so many citis’ saints or having actd in dnc o popular rights.17 And undr th nw defensors, whthr laic or clrical, th citizns conqurd ull sl-jurisdiction and sl-administration or thir olkmots.18
     Th whol procss o liration progrssd y a sris o imprcptil acts o dvotion to th common caus, accomplishd y mn who
cam out o th masss—y unknown hros whos vry nams hav not n prsrvd y history. Th wondrul movmnt o th God’s pac (treuga Dei) y which th popular masss ndavourd to put a limit to th ndlss amily uds o th nol amilis, was orn in th young towns, th ishops and th citizns trying to tnd to th nols th pac thy had stalishd within thir town walls.19 Alrady at that priod, th commrcial citis o Italy, and spcially Amal (which had its lctd consuls sinc , and rquntly changd its dogs in th tnth cntury)20 workd out th customary maritim and commrcial law which latr on cam a modl or all Europ; Ravnna laoratd its cra organization, and Milan, which had mad its rst rvolution in , cam a grat cntr o commrc, its trads njoying a ull indpndnc sinc th lvnth cntury.21 So also Brügg and Ghnt; so also svral citis o Franc in which th Mahl or forum had com a quit indpndnt institution.22 And alrady during that priod gan th work o artistic dcoration o th towns y works o architctur, which w still admir and which loudly tstiy o th intllctual movmnt o th tims. “Th asilica wr thn rnwd in almost all th univrs,” Raoul Glar wrot in his chronicl, and som o th nst monumnts o mdival architctur dat rom that priod: th wondrul old church o Brmn was uilt in th ninth cntury, Saint Marc o Vnic was nishd in , and th autiul dom o Pisa in .
In act, th intllctual movmnt which has n dscrid as th Twlh Cntury Rnaissanc23 and th Twlh Cntury Rationalism—th prcursor o th Rorm24 dat rom that priod, whn most citis wr still simpl agglomrations o small villag communitis nclosd y walls.
     Howvr, anothr lmnt, sids th villag-community principl,
was rquird to giv to ths growing cntrs o lirty and nlightnmnt th unity o thought and action, and th powrs o initiativ, which mad thir orc in th twlh and thirtnth cnturis. With th growing divrsity o occupations, cras and arts, and with th growing commrc in distant lands, som nw orm o union was rquird, and this ncssary nw lmnt was supplid y th guilds. Volums and volums hav n writtn aout ths unions which, undr th nam o guilds, rothrhoods, rindships and druzhestva, minne, artels in Russia, esnaifs in Srvia and Turky, amkari in Gorgia, and so on, took such a ormidal dvlopmnt in mdival tims and playd such an important part in th mancipation o th citis. But it took historians mor than sity yars or th univrsality o this institution and its tru charactrs wr undrstood. Only now, whn hundrds o guild statuts hav n pulishd and studid, and thir rlationship to th Roman collegiae, and th arlir unions in Grc and in India,25 is known, can w maintain with ull condnc that ths rothrhoods wr ut a urthr dvlopmnt o th sam principls which w saw at work in th gens and th villag community.
     Nothing illustrats ttr ths mdival rothrhoods than thos
tmporary guilds which wr ormd on oard ships. Whn a ship o th Hansa had accomplishd hr rst hal-day passag ar having l th port, th captain (Schier) gathrd all crw and passngrs on th dck, and hld th ollowing languag, as rportd y a contmporary:
    ‘As w ar now at th mrcy o God and th wavs,’ h said, ‘ach on
    must  qual to ach othr. And as w ar surroundd y storms,
    high wavs, pirats and othr dangrs, w must kp a strict ordr
    that w may ring our voyag to a good nd. That is why w shall
    pronounc th prayr or a good wind and good succss, and, according to marin law, w shall nam th occupirs o th judgs’ sats
    (Schöfenstellen).’ Thrupon th crw lctd a Vogt and our scabini,
    to act as thir judgs. At th nd o th voyag th Vogt and th scabini.
    adicatd thir unctions and addrssd th. ‘What has happnd
    on oard ship, w crw as ollows:—must pardon to ach othr and
    considr as dad (todt und ab sein lassen). What w hav judgd right,
    was or th sak o justic. This is why w g you all, in th nam
    o honst justic, to orgt all th animosity on may nourish against
    anothr, and to swar on rad and salt that h will not think o it in
    a ad spirit. I any on, howvr, considrs himsl wrongd, h must
    appal to th land Vogt and ask justic rom him or sunst.’ On
    landing, th Stock with th fred-nes was handd ovr to th Vogt o
    th sa-port or distriution among th poor.26
This simpl narrativ, prhaps ttr than anything ls, dpicts th spirit o th mdival guilds. Lik organizations cam into istnc whrvr a group o mn—shrmn, huntrs, travlling mrchants, uildrs, or sttld crasmn—cam togthr or a common pursuit. Thus, thr was on oard ship th naval authority o th captain; ut, or th vry succss o th common ntrpris, all mn on oard, rich and poor, mastrs and crw, captain and sailors, agrd to  quals in thir mutual rlations, to  simply mn, ound to aid ach othr and to sttl thir possil disputs or judgs lctd y all o thm. So also whn a numr o crasmn— masons, carpntrs, ston-cuttrs, tc.—cam togthr or uilding, say, a cathdral, thy all longd to a city which had its political organization, and ach o thm longd morovr to his own cra; ut thy wr unitd sids y thir common ntrpris, which thy knw ttr than any on ls, and thy joind into a ody unitd y closr, although tmporary, onds; thy oundd th guild or th uilding o th cathdral.27 W may s th sam till now in th Kaylian çof:28 th Kayls hav thir villag community; ut this union is not sucint or all political, commrcial, and prsonal nds o union, and th closr rothrhood o th çof is constitutd.
      As to th social charactrs o th mdival guild, any guild-statut may
illustrat thm. Taking, or instanc, th skraa o som arly Danish guild, w rad in it, rst, a statmnt o th gnral rothrly lings which must rign in th guild; nt com th rgulations rlativ to sl-jurisdiction in cass o quarrls arising twn two rothrs, or a rothr and a strangr; and thn, th social dutis o th rthrn ar numratd. I a rothr’s hous is urnd, or h has lost his ship, or has sufrd on a pilgrim’s voyag, all th rthrn must com to his aid. I a rothr alls dangrously ill, two rthrn must kp watch y his d till h is out o dangr, and i h dis, th rthrn must ury him—a grat afair in thos tims o pstilncs—and ollow him to th church and th grav. Ar his dath thy must provid or his childrn, i ncssary; vry on th widow coms a sistr to th guild.29
      Ths two lading aturs appard in vry rothrhood ormd or
any possil purpos. In ach cas th mmrs tratd ach othr as, and
namd ach othr, rothr and sistr;30 all wr quals or th guild. Thy ownd som “chattl” (cattl, land, uildings, placs o worship, or “stock”) in common. All rothrs took th oath o aandoning all uds o old; and, without imposing upon ach othr th oligation o nvr quarrlling again, thy agrd that no quarrl should dgnrat into a ud, or into a law-suit or anothr court than th triunal o th rothrs thmslvs. And i a rothr was involvd in a quarrl with a strangr to th guild, thy agrd to support him or ad and or good; that is, whthr h was unjustly accusd o aggrssion, or rally was th aggrssor, thy had to support him, and to ring things to a pacul nd. So long as his was not a scrt aggrssion—in which cas h would hav n tratd as an outlaw—th rothrhood stood y him.31 I th rlativs o th wrongd man wantd to rvng th ofnc at onc y a nw aggrssion, th rothrhood supplid him with a hors to run away, or with a oat, a pair o oars, a kni and a stl or striking light; i h rmaind in town, twlv rothrs accompanid him to protct him; and in th mantim thy arrangd th composition. Thy wnt to court to support y oath th truthulnss o his statmnts, and i h was ound guilty thy did not lt him go to ull ruin and com a slav through not paying th du compnsation: thy all paid it, just as th gens did in oldn tims. Only whn a rothr had rokn th aith towards his guild-rthrn, or othr popl, h was cludd rom th rothrhood “with a Nothing’s nam” (tha scal han maeles af brödrescap met nidings nafn).32
       Such wr th lading idas o thos rothrhoods which gradually
covrd th whol o mdival li. In act, w know o guilds among all possil prossions: guilds o srs,33 guilds o rmn, and guilds o oth srs and rmn; guilds calld into li or th spcial purpos o hunting, shing, or a trading pdition, and dissolvd whn th spcial purpos had n achivd; and guilds lasting or cnturis in a givn cra or trad. And, in proportion as li took an always gratr varity o pursuits, th varity in th guilds grw in proportion.      Th mdival city thus appars as a doul dration: o all hous-
holdrs unitd into small trritorial unions—th strt, th parish, th sction—and o individuals unitd y oath into guilds according to thir prossions; th ormr ing a produc o th villag-community origin o th city, whil th scond is a susqunt growth calld to li y nw conditions.
     To guarant lirty, sl-administration, and pac was th chi aim
o th mdival city. and laour, as w shall prsntly s whn spaking o th cra guilds, was its chi oundation. But “production” did not asor th whol attntion o th mdival conomist. With his practical mind, h undrstood that “consumption” must  guarantd in ordr to otain production; and thror, to provid or “th common rst ood and lodging o poor and rich alik” (gemeine notdur und gemach armer und richer) was th undamntal principl in ach city.46 Th purchas o ood supplis and othr rst ncssaris (coal, wood, tc.) or thy had rachd th markt, or altogthr in spcially avoural conditions rom which othrs would  cludd—th preempcio, in a word—was ntirly prohiitd. Evrything had to go to th markt and  ofrd thr or vry on’s purchas, till th ringing o th ll had closd th markt. hal-a-quartr) or his own us, at wholsal pric, i h did so or th nal conclusion o th argain; and rciprocally, vry akr could claim th sam i th citizn purchasd corn or r-slling it.      Howvr, all such rgulations long to latr priods o th citis’ li,
whil at an arlir priod it was th city itsl which usd to uy all ood supplis or th us o th citizns.      Th whol mattr rlativ to th communal purchass or th us o
th citizns, and th mannr in which thy usd to  mad, sms not to hav yt rcivd propr attntion rom th historians o th priod; ut thr ar hr and thr som vry intrsting acts which throw a nw light upon it.      In short, th mor w gin to know th mdival city th mor w s
that it was not simply a political organization or th protction o crtain political lirtis. It was an attmpt at organizing, on a much grandr scal
than in a villag community, a clos union or mutual aid and support, or consumption and production, and or social li altogthr, without imposing upon mn th ttrs o th Stat, ut giving ull lirty o prssion to th crativ gnius o ach sparat group o individuals in art, cras, scinc, commrc, and political organization. How ar this attmpt has n succssul will  st sn whn w hav analyzd in th nt chaptr th organization o laour in th mdival city and th rlations o th citis with th surrounding pasant population.
        H R
By creating common access to safer consumption supplies and by removing stigma and shame, harm reduction projects save lives. Projects distribute unused needles and lifesaving overdose medications, sometimes even testing substances on scene for dangerous additives. People engaged in harm reduction also support the creation
    of safer consumption spaces where people
     can use in medically assisted conditions.

M A   M C
    ()
Likeness and diversity among the medieval cities.—The cra guilds: Stateattributes in each of them.—Attitude of the city towards the peasants; attempts to free them.—The lords.—Results achieved by the medieval city: in arts, in learning.—Causes of decay.
Th mdival citis wr not organizd upon som prconcivd plan in odinc to th will o an outsid lgislator. Each o thm was a natural growth in th ull sns o th word—an always varying rsult o struggl twn various orcs which adjustd and r-adjustd thmslvs in conormity with thir rlativ nrgis, th chancs o thir conicts, and th support thy ound in thir surroundings. Thror, thr ar not two citis whos innr organization and dstinis would hav n idntical. Each on, takn sparatly, varis rom cntury to cntury. And yt, whn w cast a road glanc upon all th citis o Europ, th local and national unliknsss disappar, and w ar struck to nd among all o thm a wondrul rsmlanc, although ach has dvlopd or itsl, indpndntly rom th othrs, and in difrnt conditions. A small town in th north o Scotland, with its population o coars laourrs and shrmn; a rich city o Flandrs, with its world-wid commrc, luury, lov o amusmnt and animatd li; an Italian city nrichd y its intrcours with th East, and rding within its walls a rnd artistic tast and civilization; and a poor, chiy agricultural, city in th marsh and lak district o Russia, sm to hav littl in common. And nvrthlss, th lading lins o thir organization, and th spirit which animats thm, ar imud with a strong amily liknss. Evrywhr w s th sam drations o small communitis and guilds, th sam “su-towns” round th mothr city, th sam olkmot, and th sam insigns o its indpndnc. Th defensor o th city, undr difrnt nams and in difrnt accoutrmnts, rprsnts th sam authority and intrsts; ood supplis, laour and commrc, ar organizd on closly similar lins; innr and outr struggls ar ought with lik amitions; nay, th vry ormula usd in th struggls, as also in th annals, th ordinancs, and th rolls, ar idntical; and th architctural monumnts, whthr Gothic, Roman, or Byzantin in styl, prss th sam aspirations and th sam idals; thy ar concivd and uilt in th sam way. Many dissmlancs ar mr difrncs o ag, and thos disparitis twn
sistr citis which ar ral ar rpatd in difrnt parts o Europ. Th unity o th lading ida and th idntity o origin mak up or difrncs o climat, gographical situation, walth, languag and rligion. This is why w can spak o the mdival city as o a wll-dnd phas o civilization; and whil vry rsarch insisting upon local and individual difrncs is most wlcom, w may still indicat th chi lins o dvlopmnt which ar common to all citis.1
     Thr is no dout that th protction which usd to  accordd to th
markt-plac rom th arlist ararian tims has playd an important, though not an clusiv, part in th mancipation o th mdival city. Th arly ararians knw no trad within thir villag communitis; thy tradd with strangrs only, at crtain dnit spots, on crtain dtrmind days. And, in ordr that th strangr might com to th artr-plac without risk o ing slain or som ud which might  running twn two kins, th markt was always placd undr th spcial protction o all kins. It was inviolal, lik th plac o worship undr th shadow o which it was hld. With th Kayls it is still anaya, lik th ootpath along which womn carry watr rom th wll; nithr must  troddn upon in arms, vn during intr-trial wars. In mdival tims th markt univrsally njoyd th sam protction.2 No ud could  proscutd on th plac whrto popl cam to trad, nor within a crtain radius rom it; and i a quarrl aros in th motly crowd o uyrs and sllrs, it had to  rought or thos undr whos protction th markt stood—th community’s triunal, or th ishop’s, th lord’s, or th king’s judg. A strangr who cam to trad was a gust, and h wnt on undr this vry nam. Evn th lord who had no scrupls aout roing a mrchant on th high road, rspctd th Weichbild, that is, th pol which stood in th markt-plac and or ithr th king’s arms, or a glov, or th imag o th local saint, or simply a cross, according to whthr th markt was undr th protction o th king, th lord, th local church, or th olkmot—th vyeche.3
     It is asy to undrstand how th sl-jurisdiction o th city could
dvlop out o th spcial jurisdiction in th markt-plac, whn this last right was concdd, willingly or not, to th city itsl. And such an origin o th city’s lirtis, which can  tracd in vry many cass, ncssarily laid a spcial stamp upon thir susqunt dvlopmnt. It gav a prdominanc to th trading part o th community. Th urghrs who possssd a hous in th city at th tim ing, and wr co-ownrs in th town-lands, constitutd vry on a mrchant guild which hld in its hands th city’s trad; and although at th outst vry urghr, rich and poor, could mak part o th mrchant guild, and th trad itsl sms to hav n carrid
on or th ntir city y its trusts, th guild gradually cam a sort o privilgd ody. It jalously prvntd th outsidrs who soon gan to ock into th r citis rom ntring th guild, and kpt th advantags rsulting rom trad or th w “amilis” which had n urghrs at th tim o th mancipation. Thr vidntly was a dangr o a mrchant oligarchy ing thus constitutd. But alrady in th tnth, and still mor during th two nt cnturis, th chi cras, also organizd in guilds, wr powrul nough to chck th oligarchic tndncis o th mrchants.
     Th cra guild was thn a common sllr o its produc and a common
uyr o th raw matrials, and its mmrs wr mrchants and manual workrs at th sam tim. Thror, th prdominanc takn y th old cra guilds rom th vry ginnings o th r city li guarantd to manual laour th high position which it arwards occupid in th city.4 In act, in a mdival city manual laour was no tokn o inriority; it or, on th contrary, tracs o th high rspct it had n kpt in in th villag community. Manual laour in a “mystry” was considrd as a pious duty towards th citizns: a pulic unction (Amt), as honoural as any othr. An ida o “justic” to th community, o “right” towards oth producr and consumr, which would sm so travagant now, pntratd production and chang. Th tannr’s, th coopr’s, or th shomakr’s work must  “just,” air, thy wrot in thos tims. Wood, lathr or thrad which ar usd y th artisan must  “right”; rad must  akd “in justic,” and so on. Transport this languag into our prsnt li, and it would sm afctd and unnatural; ut it was natural and unafctd thn, caus th mdival artisan did not produc or an unknown uyr, or to throw his goods into an unknown markt. H producd or his guild rst; or a roth- rhood o mn who knw ach othr, knw th tchnics o th cra, and, in naming th pric o ach product, could apprciat th skill displayd in its arication or th laour stowd upon it. Thn th guild, not th sparat producr, ofrd th goods or sal in th community, and this last, in its turn, ofrd to th rothrhood o allid communitis thos goods which wr portd, and assumd rsponsiility or thir quality. With such an organization, it was th amition o ach cra not to ofr goods o inrior quality, and tchnical dcts or adultrations cam a mattr concrning th whol community, caus, an ordinanc says, “thy would dstroy pulic condnc.”5 Production ing thus a social duty, placd undr th control o th whol amitas, manual laour could not all into th dgradd condition which it occupis now, so long as th r city was living.
     A difrnc twn mastr and apprntic, or twn mastr and
workr (compayne, Geselle), istd ut in th mdival citis rom thir

     Thr was not much room or hird work in th arly ourishing
priods o th mdival citis, still lss or individual hirlings. Th work o th wavrs, th archrs, th smiths, th akrs, and so on, was prormd or th cra and th city; and whn crasmn wr hird in th uilding trads, thy workd as tmporary corporations (as thy still do in th Russian artels), whos work was paid en bloc. Work or a mastr gan to multiply only latr on; ut vn in this cas th workr was paid ttr than h is paid now, vn in this country, and vry much ttr than h usd to  paid all ovr Europ in th rst hal o this cntury. Thorold Rogrs has amiliarizd English radrs with this ida; ut th sam is tru or th Continnt as wll, as is shown y th rsarchs o Falk and Schönrg, and y many occasional indications. Evn in th nth cntury a mason, a carpntr, or a smith workr would  paid at Amins our sols a day, which corrspondd to orty-ight pounds o rad, or to th ighth part o a small o (bouvard). In Saony, th salary o th Geselle in th uilding trad was such that, to put it in Falk’s words, h could uy with his si days’ wags thr shp and on pair o shos.6 Th donations o workrs (Geselle) to cathdrals also ar tstimony o thir rlativ wll-ing, to say nothing o th glorious donations o crtain cra guilds nor o what thy usd to spnd in stivitis and pagants.7 In act, th mor w larn aout th mdival city, th mor w ar convincd that at no tim has laour njoyd such conditions o prosprity and such rspct as whn city li stood at its highst.
     Mor than that; not only many aspirations o our modrn radicals wr
alrady ralizd in th middl ags, ut much o what is dscrid now as Utopian was accptd thn as a mattr o act. W ar laughd at whn w say that work must  plasant, ut—“vry on must  plasd with his work,” a mdival Kuttnrg ordinanc says, “and no on shall, whil doing nothing (mit nichts thun), appropriat or himsl what othrs hav producd y application and work, caus laws must  a shild or application and work.”8 And amidst all prsnt talk aout an ight hours’ day, it may  wll to rmmr an ordinanc o Frdinand th First rlativ to th Imprial coal mins, which sttld th minr’s day at ight hours, “as it usd
to  o old” (wie vor Alters herkommen), and work on Saturday arnoon was prohiitd. Longr hours wr vry rar, w ar told y Janssn, whil shortr hours wr o common occurrnc. In this country, in th nth cntury, Rogrs says, “th workmn workd only orty-ight hours a wk.”9 Th Saturday hal-holiday, too, which w considr as a modrn conqust, was in rality an old mdival institution; it was athing-tim or a grat part o th community, whil Wdnsday arnoon was athing-tim or th Geselle.10 And although school mals did not ist—proaly caus no childrn wnt hungry to school—a distriution o ath-mony to th childrn whos parnts ound diculty in providing it was haitual in svral placs As to Laour Congrsss, thy also wr a rgular atur o th middls ags. In som parts o Grmany crasmn o th sam trad, longing to difrnt communs, usd to com togthr vry yar to discuss qustions rlativ to thir trad, th yars o apprnticship, th wandring yars, th wags, and so on; and in , th Hansatic towns ormally rcognizd th right o th cras to com togthr at priodical congrsss, and to tak any rsolutions, so long as thy wr not contrary to th citis’ rolls, rlativ to th quality o goods. Such Laour Congrsss, partly intrnational lik th Hansa itsl, ar known to hav n hld y akrs, oundrs, smiths, tannrs, sword-makrs and cask-makrs.11
     Th cra organization rquird, o cours, a clos suprvision o th
crasmn y th guild, and spcial jurats wr always nominatd or that purpos. But it is most rmarkal that, so long as th citis livd thir r li, no complaints wr hard aout th suprvision; whil, ar th Stat had stppd in, conscating th proprty o th guilds and dstroying thir indpndnc in avour o its own uraucracy, th complaints cam simply countlss.12 On th othr hand, th immnsity o progrss ralizd in all arts undr th mdival guild systm is th st proo that th systm was no hindranc to individual initiativ.13 Th act is, that th mdival guild, lik th mdival parish, “strt,” or “quartr,” was not a ody o citizns, placd undr th control o Stat unctionaris; it was a union o all mn connctd with a givn trad: jurat uyrs o raw produc, sllrs o manuacturd goods, and artisans—mastrs, “compayns,” and apprntics. For th innr organization o th trad its assmly was sov- rign, so long as it did not hampr th othr guilds, in which cas th mattr was rought or th guild o th guilds—th city. But thr was in it somthing mor than that. It had its own sl-jurisdiction, its own military orc, its own gnral assmlis, its own traditions o struggls, glory, and indpndnc, its own rlations with othr guilds o th sam trad in othr citis: it had, in a word, a ull organic li which could only
rsult rom th intgrality o th vital unctions. Whn th town was calld to arms, th guild appard as a sparat company (Schaar), armd with its own arms (or its own guns, lovingly dcoratd y th guild, at a su- squnt poch), undr its own sl-lctd commandrs. It was, in a word, as indpndnt a unit o th dration as th rpulic o Uri or Gnva was y yars ago in th Swiss Condration. So that, to compar it with a modrn trad union, divstd o all attriuts o Stat sovrignty, and rducd to a coupl o unctions o scondary importanc, is as unrasonal as to compar Flornc or Brügg with a Frnch commun vgtating undr th Cod Napoléon, or with a Russian town placd undr Cathrin th Scond’s municipal law. Both hav lctd mayors, and th lattr has also its cra corporations; ut th difrnc is—all th difrnc that ists twn Flornc and Fontnay-ls-Ois or Tsarvokokshaisk, or twn a Vntian dog and a modrn mayor who lis his hat or th sous-préfet’s clrk.
     Th mdival guilds wr capal o maintaining thir indpndnc;
and, latr on, spcially in th ourtnth cntury, whn, in consqunc o svral causs which shall prsntly  indicatd, th old municipal li undrwnt a dp modication, th youngr cras provd strong nough to conqur thir du shar in th managmnt o th city afairs. Th masss, organizd in “minor” arts, ros to wrst th powr out o th hands o a growing oligarchy, and mostly succdd in this task, opning again a nw ra o prosprity. Tru, that in som citis th uprising was crushd in lood, and mass dcapitations o workrs ollowd, as was th cas in Paris in , and in Cologn in . In such cass th city’s lirtis rapidly ll into dcay, and th city was gradually sudud y th cntral authority. But th majority o th towns had prsrvd nough o vitality to com out o th turmoil with a nw li and vigour.14 A nw priod o rjuvnscnc was thir rward. Nw li was inusd, and it ound its prssion in splndid architctural monumnts, in a nw priod o prosprity, in a suddn progrss o tchnics and invntion, and in a nw intllctual movmnt lading to th Rnaissanc and to th Rormation.
     Th li o a mdival city was a succssion o hard attls to conqur
lirty and to maintain it. Tru, that a strong and tnacious rac o urgh- rs had dvlopd during thos rc contsts; tru, that lov and worship o th mothr city had n rd y ths struggls, and that th grand things achivd y th mdival communs wr a dirct outcom o that lov. Vry w citis had succdd, undr a concurrnc
o avoural circumstancs, in otaining lirty at on strok, and ths w mostly lost it qually asily; whil th grat numr had to ght y or a hundrd yars in succssion, on mor, or thir rights to r li had n rcognizd, and anothr hundrd yars to ound thir lirty on a rm asis—th twlh cntury chartrs thus ing ut on o th stpping-stons to rdom.15 In rality, th mdival city was a ortid oasis amidst a country plungd into udal sumission, and it had to mak room or itsl y th orc o its arms. In consqunc o th causs riy alludd to in th prcding chaptr, ach villag community had gradually alln undr th yok o som lay or clrical lord. His hous had grown to  a castl, and his rothrs-in-arms wr now th scum o advnturrs, always rady to plundr th pasants. In addition to thr days a wk which th pasants had to work or th lord, thy had also to ar all sorts o actions or th right to sow and to crop, to  gay or sad, to liv, to marry, or to di. And, worst o all, thy wr continually plundrd y th armd rors o som nighouring lord, who chos to considr thm as thir mastr’s kin, and to tak upon thm, and upon thir cattl and crops, th rvng or a ud h was ghting against thir ownr. Evry madow, vry ld, vry rivr, and road around th city, and vry man upon th land was undr som lord.
      Th hatrd o th urghrs towards th udal arons has ound a most
charactristic prssion in th wording o th difrnt chartrs which thy complld thm to sign. Hinrich V. is mad to sign in th chartr grantd to Spir in , that h rs th urghrs rom “th horril and cra- l law o mortmain, through which th town has n sunk into dpst povrty” (von dem scheusslichen und nichtswürdigen Gesetze, welches gemein Budel genannt wird, Kallsn, i. ). Th coutume o Bayonn, writtn aout , contains such passags as ths: “Th popl is antrior to th lords. It is th popl, mor numrous than all othrs, who, dsirous o pac, has mad th lords or ridling and knocking down th powrul ons,” and so on (Giry, Établissements de Rouen, i. , Quotd y Luchair, ). A chartr sumittd or King Rort’s signatur is qually charactristic. H is mad to say in it: “I shall ro no on nor othr animals. I shall siz no mrchants, nor tak thir monys, nor impos ransom. From Lady Day to th All Saints’ Day I shall siz no hors, nor mar, nor oals, in th madows. I shall not urn th mills, nor ro th our . . . I shall ofr no protction to thivs,” tc. (Pstr has pulishd that documnt, rproducd y Luchair). Th chartr “grantd” y th Bsançon Archishop Hugus, in which h has n complld to numrat all th mischis du to his mortmain rights, is qually charactristic.16 And so on.
     Frdom could not  maintaind in such surroundings, and th citis
wr complld to carry on th war outsid thir walls. Th urghrs snt out missaris to lad rvolt in th villags; thy rcivd villags into thir corporations, and thy wagd dirct war against th nols. In Italy, whr th land was thickly sprinkld with udal castls, th war assumd hroic proportions, and was ought with a strn acrimony on oth sids. Flornc sustaind or svnty-svn yars a succssion o loody wars, in ordr to r its contado rom th nols; ut whn th conqust had n accomplishd (in ) all had to gin anw. Th nols rallid; thy constitutd thir own lagus in opposition to th lagus o th towns, and, rciving rsh support rom ithr th Empror or th Pop, thy mad th war last or anothr  yars. Th sam took plac in Rom, in Lomardy, all ovr Italy.
     Prodigis o valour, audacity, and tnaciousnss wr displayd y th
citizns in ths wars. But th ows and th hatchts o th arts and cras had not always th uppr hand in thir ncountrs with th armour-clad knights, and many castls withstood th ingnious sig-machinry and th prsvranc o th citizns. Som citis, lik Flornc, Bologna, and many towns in Franc, Grmany, and Bohmia, succdd in mancipating th surrounding villags, and thy wr rwardd or thir forts y an traordinary prosprity and tranquillity. But vn hr, and still mor in th lss strong or lss impulsiv towns, th mrchants and artisans, haustd y war, and misundrstanding thir own intrsts, argaind ovr th pasants’ hads. Thy complld th lord to swar allgianc to th city; his country castl was dismantld, and h agrd to uild a hous and to rsid in th city, o which h cam a co-urghr (com-bourgeois, con-cittadino); ut h maintaind in rturn most o his rights upon th pasants, who only won a partial rli rom thir urdns. Th urghr could not undrstand that qual rights o citiznship might  grantd to th pasant upon whos ood supplis h had to rly, and a dp rnt was tracd twn town and villag. In som cass th pasants simply changd ownrs, th city uying out th arons’ rights and slling thm in shars to hr own citizns.17 Srdom was maintaind, and only much latr on, towards th nd o th thirtnth cntury, it was th cra rvolution which undrtook to put an nd to it, and aolishd prsonal srvitud, ut dispossssd at th sam tim th srs o th land.18 It hardly nd  addd that th atal rsults o such policy wr soon lt y th citis thmslvs; th country cam th city’s nmy.
     Th war against th castls had anothr ad fct. It involvd th citis
in a long succssion o mutual wars, which hav givn origin to th thory,
till latly in vogu, namly, that th towns lost thir indpndnc through thir own jalousis and mutual ghts. Th imprialist historians hav spcially supportd this thory, which, howvr, is vry much undrmind now y modrn rsarch. It is crtain that in Italy citis ought ach othr with a stuorn animosity, ut nowhr ls did such contsts attain th sam proportions; and in Italy itsl th city wars, spcially thos o th arlir priod, had thir spcial causs. Thy wr (as was alrady shown y Sismondi and Frrari) a mr continuation o th war against th castls— th r municipal and drativ principl unavoidaly ntring into a rc contst with udalism, imprialism, and papacy. Many towns which had ut partially shakn of th yok o th ishop, th lord, or th Empror, wr simply drivn against th r citis y th nols, th Empror, and Church, whos policy was to divid th citis and to arm thm against ach othr. Ths spcial circumstancs (partly rctd on to Grmany also) plain why th Italian towns, som o which sought support with th Empror to comat th Pop, whil th othrs sought support rom th Church to rsist th Empror, wr soon dividd into a Gilin and a Gul camp, and why th sam division appard in ach sparat city.19
       Th immns conomical progrss ralizd y most Italian citis just
at th tim whn ths wars wr hottst,20 and th alliancs so asily concludd twn towns, still ttr charactriz thos struggls and urthr undrmin th aov thory. Alrady in th yars – pow- rul lagus cam into istnc; and a w yars latr, whn Frdrick Bararossa invadd Italy and, supportd y th nols and som rtardatory citis, marchd against Milan, popular nthusiasm was rousd in many towns y popular prachrs. Crma, Piacnza, Brscia, Tortona, tc., wnt to th rscu; th annrs o th guilds o Vrona, Padua, Vicnza, and Trvisa oatd sid y sid in th citis’ camp against th annrs o th Empror and th nols. Nt yar th Lomardian Lagu cam into istnc, and sity yars latr w s it rinorcd y many othr citis, and orming a lasting organization which had hal o its dral warchst in Gnoa and th othr hal in Vnic.21 In Tuscany, Flornc hadd anothr powrul lagu, to which Lucca, Bologna, Pistoia, tc., longd, and which playd an important part in crushing down th nols in middl Italy, whil smallr lagus wr o common occurrnc.       Th worst was, that th growing autocracis ound support in th divisions which had grown within th citis thmslvs. Th undamntal ida
o th mdival city was grand, ut it was not wid nough. Mutual aid and support cannot  limitd to a small association; thy must sprad to its surroundings, or ls th surroundings will asor th association. For th ormr, all nts rom communal trad and communal lands wr rsrvd, and nothing was l or th lattr ut th right o rly using th skill o thir own hands.       Th sam division took plac twn th city propr and th surrounding villags. Th commun had wll trid to r th pasants, ut
hr wars against th lords cam, as alrady mntiond, wars or ring th city itsl rom th lords, rathr than or ring th pasants. Sh l to th lord his rights ovr th villins, on condition that h would molst th city no mor and would com co-urghr. But th nols “adoptd”
y th city, and now rsiding within its walls, simply carrid on th old war within th vry prcincts o th city. Drawing larg incoms rom th stats thy had still rtaind, thy surroundd thmslvs with numrous clints and udalizd th customs and haits o th city itsl. By cooperating in the face of individual pressures, when tenants all withhold rent, they can achieve better living conditions and lessen precarity. People suffering under landlords can come together to resist their police stooges and take
     back or open up buildings for residents.

## O

Popular revolts at the beginning of the State-period.—Mutual aid institutions of the present time.—The village community; its struggles for resisting its abolition by the State.—Habits derived from the village-community life, retained in our modern villages.—Switzerland, France, Germany, Russia.
Th mutual-aid tndncy in man has so rmot an origin, and is so dply intrwovn with all th past volution o th human rac, that it has n maintaind y mankind up to th prsnt tim, notwithstanding all vicissituds o history. It was chiy volvd during priods o pac and prosprity; ut whn vn th gratst calamitis ll mn—whn whol countris wr laid wast y wars, and whol populations wr dcimatd y misry, or groand undr th yok o tyranny—th sam tndncy continud to liv in th villags and among th poorr classs in th towns; it still kpt thm togthr, and in th long run it ractd vn upon thos ruling, ghting, and dvastating minoritis which dismissd it as sntimntal nonsns. And whnvr mankind had to work out a nw social organization, adaptd to a nw phasis o dvlopmnt, its constructiv gnius always drw th lmnts and th inspiration or th nw dpartur rom that sam vr-living tndncy. Nw conomical and social institutions, in so ar as thy wr a cration o th masss, nw thical systms, and nw rligions, all hav originatd rom th sam sourc, and th thical progrss o our rac, viwd in its road lins, appars as a gradual tnsion o th mutual-aid principls rom th tri to always largr and largr agglom- rations, so as to nally mrac on day th whol o mankind, without rspct to its divrs crds, languags, and racs.
     Ar having passd through th savag tri, and nt through th
villag community, th Europans cam to work out in mdival tims a nw orm o organization, which had th advantag o allowing grat latitud or individual initiativ, whil it largly rspondd at th sam tim to man’s nd o mutual support. A dration o villag communitis, covrd y a ntwork o guilds and ratrnitis, was calld into istnc in th mdival citis. Th immns rsults achivd undr this nw orm o union—in wll-ing or all, in industris, art, scinc, and commrc— wr discussd at som lngth in two prcding chaptrs, and an attmpt was also mad to show why, towards th nd o th nth cntury, th

     For th nt thr cnturis th Stats, oth on th Continnt and

Middl Europ. Evn th chi dats o th grat assaults upon th pasant lands ar th sam. Th sizur o th communal lands y th lords also gan in th nth cntury, ar th dat o th pasant insurrction o —as sn rom Rossus’s Historia and rom a statut o Hnry th Svnth, in which ths sizurs ar spokn o undr th hading o “normits and myschs as  hurtull . . . to th common wl.”9 Latr on th Grat Inqust, undr Hnry th Eighth, was
gun, as is known, in ordr to put a stop to th nclosur o communal lands, ut it ndd in a sanction o what had n don.10 Th communal lands continud to  pryd upon, and th pasants wr drivn rom th land. But it was spcially sinc th middl o th ightnth cntury that, in England as vrywhr ls, it cam part o a systmatic policy to simply wd out all tracs o communal ownrship; and th wondr is not that it has disappard, ut that it could  maintaind, vn in England, so as to  “gnrally prvalnt so lat as th grandathrs o this gnration.”11 Th vry ojct o th Enclosur Acts, as shown y Mr. Sohm, was to rmov this systm,12 and it was so wll rmovd y th narly our thousand Acts passd twn  and  that only aint tracs o it rmain now. Th land o th villag communitis was takn y th lords, and th appropriation was sanctiond y Parliamnt in ach sparat cas.
     In Grmany, in Austria, in Blgium th villag community was also
dstroyd y th Stat. Instancs o commonrs thmslvs dividing thir lands wr rar,13 whil vrywhr th Stats corcd thm to norc th division, or simply avourd th privat appropriation o thir lands. Th last low to communal ownrship in Middl Europ also dats rom th middl o th ightnth cntury. In Austria shr orc was usd y th Govrnmnt, in , to compl th communs to divid thir lands—a spcial commission ing nominatd two yars latr or that purpos. In Prussia Frdrick th Scond, in svral o his ordinancs (in , , , and ), rcommndd to th Justizcollegien to norc th division. In Silsia a spcial rsolution was issud to srv that aim in . Th sam took plac in Blgium, and, as th communs did not oy, a law was issud in  mpowring th Govrnmnt to uy communal madows in ordr to sll thm in rtail, and to mak a orcd sal o th communal land whn thr was a would- uyr or it.14
     In short, to spak o th natural dath o th villag communitis in
virtu o conomical laws is as grim a jok as to spak o th natural dath o soldirs slaughtrd on a attlld. Th act was simply this: Th villag communitis had livd or ovr a thousand yars; and whr and whn th pasants wr not ruind y wars and actions thy stadily improvd thir mthods o cultur. But as th valu o land was incrasing, in consqunc o th growth o industris, and th noility had acquird, undr th Stat organization, a powr which it nvr had had undr th udal systm, it took possssion o th st parts o th communal lands, and did its st to dstroy th communal institutions.
     Howvr, th villag-community institutions so wll rspond to th
nds and concptions o th tillrs o th soil that, in spit o all, Europ
is up to this dat covrd with living survivals o th villag communitis, and Europan country li is prmatd with customs and haits dating rom th community priod. Evn in England, notwithstanding all th drastic masurs takn against th old ordr o things, it prvaild as lat as th ginning o th nintnth cntury. Mr. Gomm—on o th vry w English scholars who hav paid attntion to th sujct—shows in his work that many tracs o th communal possssion o th soil ar ound in Scotland, “runrig” tnancy having n maintaind in Forarshir up to , whil in crtain villags o Invrnss th custom was, up to , to plough th land or th whol community, without laving any oundaris, and to allot it ar th ploughing was don. In Kilmori th allotmnt and r-allotmnt o th lds was in ull vigour “till th last twnty-v yars,” and th Crors’ Commission ound it still in vigour in crtain islands.15 In Irland th systm prvaild up to th grat amin; and as to England, Marshall’s works, which passd unnoticd until Nass and Sir Hnry Main drw attntion to thm, lav no dout as to th villag-community systm having n widly sprad, in narly all English countis, at th ginning o th nintnth cntury.16 No mor than twnty yars ago Sir Hnry Main was “gratly surprisd at th numr o instancs o anormal proprty rights, ncssarily implying th ormr istnc o collctiv ownrship and joint cultivation,” which a comparativly ri inquiry rought undr his notic.17 And, communal institutions having prsistd so lat as that, a grat numr o mutual-aid haits and customs would undoutdly  discovrd in English villags i th writrs o this country only paid attntion to villag li.18
     As to th Continnt, w nd th communal institutions ully aliv in
many parts o Franc, Switzrland, Grmany, Italy, th Scandinavian lands, and Spain, to say nothing o Eastrn Europ; th villag li in ths countris is prmatd with communal haits and customs; and almost vry yar th Continntal litratur is nrichd y srious works daling with this and connctd sujcts. I must, thror, limit my illustrations to th most typical instancs. Switzrland is undoutdly on o thm. Not only th v rpulics o Uri, Schwytz, Appnzll, Glarus, and Untrwaldn hold thir lands as undividd stats, and ar govrnd y thir popular olkmots, ut in all othr cantons too th villag communitis rmain in possssion o a wid sl-govrnmnt, and own larg parts o th Fdral trritory.19 Two-thirds o all th Alpin madows and two-thirds o all th orsts o Switzrland ar until now communal land; and a considral numr o lds, orchards, vinyards, pat ogs, quarris, and so on, ar ownd in common. In th Vaud, whr all th housholdrs continu to
tak part in th dlirations o thir lctd communal councils, th communal spirit is spcially aliv. Towards th nd o th wintr all th young mn o ach villag go to stay a w days in th woods, to ll timr and to ring it down th stp slops toogganing way, th timr and th ul wood ing dividd among all housholds or sold or thir nt. Ths cursions ar ral êts o manly laour. On th anks o Lak Lman part o th work rquird to kp up th trracs o th vinyards is still don in common; and in th spring, whn th thrmomtr thratns to all low zro or sunris, th watchman waks up all housholdrs, who light rs o straw and dung and protct thir vin-trs rom th rost y an articial cloud. In narly all cantons th villag communitis possss socalld Bürgernutzen—that is, thy hold in common a numr o cows, in ordr to supply ach amily with uttr; or thy kp communal lds or vinyards, o which th produc is dividd twn th urghrs, or thy rnt thir land or th nt o th community.20
     It may  takn as a rul that whr th communs hav rtaind a wid
sphr o unctions, so as to  living parts o th national organism, and whr thy hav not n rducd to shr misry, thy nvr ail to tak good car o thir lands. Accordingly th communal stats in Switzrland strikingly contrast with th misral stat o “commons” in this country. Th communal orsts in th Vaud and th Valais ar admiraly managd, in conormity with th ruls o modrn orstry. Elswhr th “strips” o communal lds, which chang ownrs undr th systm o r-allotmnt, ar vry wll manurd, spcially as thr is no lack o madows and cattl. Th high lvl madows ar wll kpt as a rul, and th rural roads ar cllnt.21 And whn w admir th Swiss châlet, th mountain road, th pasants’ cattl, th trracs o vinyards, or th school-hous in Switzrland, w must kp in mind that without th timr or th châlet ing takn rom th communal woods and th ston rom th communal quarris, without th cows ing kpt on th communal madows, and th roads ing mad and th school-houss uilt y communal work, thr would  littl to admir.
     It hardly nd  said that a grat numr o mutual-aid haits and
customs continu to prsist in th Swiss villags. Th vning gathrings or shlling walnuts, which tak plac in turns in ach houshold; th vning partis or swing th dowry o th girl who is going to marry; th calling o “aids” or uilding th houss and taking in th crops, as wll as or all sorts o work which may  rquird y on o th commonrs; th custom o changing childrn rom on canton to th othr, in ordr to mak thm larn two languags, Frnch and Grman; and so on—all ths ar quit haitual;22 whil, on th othr sid, divrs modrn rquirmnts
ar mt in th sam spirit. Thus in Glarus most o th Alpin madows hav n sold during a tim o calamity; ut th communs still continu to uy ld land, and ar th nwly ought lds hav n l in th possssion o sparat commonrs or tn, twnty, or thirty yars, as th cas might , thy rturn to th common stock, which is r-allottd according to th nds o all. A grat numr o small associations ar ormd to produc som o th ncssaris or li—rad, chs, and win—y common work,  it only on a limitd scal; and agricultural co-opration altogthr sprads in Switzrland with th gratst as. Associations ormd twn tn to thirty pasants, who uy madows and lds in common, and cultivat thm as co-ownrs, ar o common occurrnc; whil dairy associations or th sal o milk, uttr, and chs ar organizd vrywhr. In act, Switzrland was th irthplac o that orm o co-opration. It ofrs, mor- ovr, an immns ld or th study o all sorts o small and larg socitis, ormd or th satisaction o all sorts o modrn wants. In crtain parts o Switzrland on nds in almost vry villag a numr o associations—or protction rom r, or oating, or maintaining th quays on th shors o a lak, or th supply o watr, and so on; and th country is covrd with socitis o archrs, sharpshootrs, topographrs, ootpath plorrs, and th lik, originatd rom modrn militarism.
     Switzrland is, howvr, y no mans an cption in Europ, caus
th sam institutions and haits ar ound in th villags o Franc, o Italy, o Grmany, o Dnmark, and so on. W hav just sn what has n don y th rulrs o Franc in ordr to dstroy th villag community and to gt hold o its lands; ut notwithstanding all that, on-tnth part o th whol trritory availal or cultur, i.. ,, acrs, including on-hal o all th natural madows and narly a h part o all th orsts o th country, rmain in communal possssion. Th woods supply th communrs with ul, and th timr wood is cut, mostly y communal work, with all dsiral rgularity; th grazing lands ar r or th commonrs’ cattl; and what rmains o communal lds is allottd and r-allottd in crtain parts Ardnns—in th usual o Franc—namly, in th way.23
     Ths additional sourcs o supply, which aid th poorr pasants to
pass through a yar o ad crops without parting with thir small plots o land and without running into irrdmal dts, hav crtainly thir importanc or oth th agricultural laourrs and th narly thr millions o small pasant propritors. It is vn doutul whthr small pasant propritorship could  maintaind without ths additional rsourcs. But th thical importanc o th communal possssions, small as thy ar, is still gratr than thir conomical valu. Thy maintain in villag li a
nuclus o customs and haits o mutual aid which undoutdly acts as a mighty chck upon th dvlopmnt o rcklss individualism and grdinss, which small land-ownrship is only too pron to dvlop. Mutual aid in all possil circumstancs o villag li is part o th routin li in all parts o th country. Evrywhr w mt, undr difrnt nams, with th charroi, i.. th r aid o th nighours or taking in a crop, or vintag, or or uilding a hous; vrywhr w nd th sam vning gathrings as hav just n mntiond in Switzrland; and vrywhr th common- rs associat or all sorts o work. Such haits ar mntiond y narly all thos who hav writtn upon Frnch villag li. But it will prhaps  ttr to giv in this plac som astracts rom lttrs which I hav just rcivd rom a rind o min whom I hav askd to communicat to m his osrvations on this sujct. Thy com rom an agd man who or yars has n th mayor o his commun in South Franc (in Arièg); th acts h mntions ar known to him rom long yars o prsonal osrvation, and thy hav th advantag o coming rom on nighourhood instad o ing skimmd rom a larg ara. Som o thm may sm triing, ut as a whol thy dpict quit a littl world o villag li. My rind writs:
    In svral communs in our nighourhood, th old custom o
     l’emprount is in vigour. Whn many hands ar rquird in a métairie
    or rapidly making som work—dig out potatos or mow th grass—
    th youth o th nighourhood is convokd; young mn and girls
    com in numrs, mak it gaily and or nothing; and in th vning,
    ar a gay mal, thy danc.
        In th sam communs, whn a girl is going to marry, th girls
    o th nighourhood com to aid in swing th dowry. In svral
    communs th womn still continu to spin a good dal. Whn th
    winding of has to  don in a amily it is don in on vning—all
    rinds ing convokd or that work. In many communs o th
    Arièg and othr parts o th south-wst th shlling o th Indian
    corn-shavs is also don y all th nighours. Thy ar tratd
    with chstnuts and win, and th young popl danc ar th work
    has n don. Th sam custom is practicd or making nut oil and
    crushing hmp. In th commun o L. th sam is don or ringing
    in th corn crops. Ths days o hard work com fête days, as th

    is givn; all do it or ach othr.24
        In th commun o S. th common grazing-land is vry yar

        In th commun o M. th orty to y small shp ocks o th
    commonrs ar rought togthr and dividd into thr or our ocks

    to srv as shphrd.

    common y svral housholds; th n to twnty prsons rquird
    to srv th machin ing supplid y all th amilis. Thr othr
    thrshing machins hav n ought and ar rntd out y thir

    usual way.
        In our commun o R. w had to rais th wall o th cmtry.
    Hal o th mony which was rquird or uying lim and or th

    th commun.
Two rsidnts o th sam nighourhood, qustiond y my rind, add th ollowing:—
    At O. a w yars ago thr was no mill. Th commun has uilt on,
    lvying a ta upon th commonrs. As to th millr, thy dcidd, in
    ordr to avoid rauds and partiality, that h should  paid two rancs
    or ach rad-atr, and th corn  ground r.
       At St. G. w pasants ar insurd against r. Whn a conagration has takn plac—so it was latly—all giv somthing to th
    amily which has sufrd rom it—a chaldron, a d-cloth, a chair,
    and so on—and a modst houshold is thus rconstitutd. All th

    lodgd r y th nighours.
Such haits o mutual support—o which many mor ampls could  givn—undoutdly account or th asinss with which th Frnch pasants associat or using, in turn, th plough with its tam o horss, th win-prss, and th thrshing machin, whn thy ar kpt in th villag y
on o thm only, as wll as or th prormanc o all sorts o rural work in common. Canals wr maintaind, orsts wr clard, trs wr plantd, and marshs wr draind y th villag communitis rom tim imm- morial; and th sam continus still. Quit latly, in La Borne o Lozèr arrn hills wr turnd into rich gardns y communal work. “Th soil was rought on mn’s acks; trracs wr mad and plantd with chstnut trs, pach trs, and orchards, and watr was rought or irrigation in canals two or thr mils long.” Just now thy hav dug a nw canal, lvn mils in lngth.25
      To th sam spirit is also du th rmarkal succss latly otaind
y th syndicats agricoles, or pasants’ and armrs’ associations. It was not until  that associations o mor than nintn prsons wr prmittd in Franc, and I nd not say that whn this “dangrous primnt” was vnturd upon—so it was styld in th Chamrs—all du “prcautions” which unctionaris can invnt wr takn. Notwithstanding all that, Franc gins to  covrd with syndicats. At th outst thy wr only ormd or uying manurs and sds, alsication having attaind colossal proportions in ths two ranchs;26 ut gradually thy tndd thir unctions in various dirctions, including th sal o agricultural produc and prmannt improvmnts o th land. In South Franc th ravags o th phyllora hav calld into istnc a grat numr o win-growrs’ associations. Tn to thirty growrs orm a syndicat, uy a stam ngin or pumping watr, and mak th ncssary arrangmnts or inundating thir vinyards in turn.27 Nw associations or protcting th land rom inundations, or irrigation purposs, and or maintaining canals ar continually ormd, and th unanimity o all pasants o a nighourhood, which is rquird y law, is no ostacl. Elswhr w hav th fruitières, or dairy associations, in som o which all uttr and chs is dividd in qual parts, irrspctiv o th yild o ach cow. In th Arièg w nd an association o ight sparat communs or th common cultur o thir lands, which thy hav put togthr; syndicats or r mdical aid hav n ormd in  communs out o  in th sam dpartmnt; associations o consumrs aris in connction with th syndicats; and so on.28 “Quit a rvolution is going on in our villags,” Alrd Baudrillart writs, “through ths associations, which tak in ach rgion thir own spcial charactrs.
     “Vry much th sam must  said o Grmany. Whrvr th pasants
could rsist th plundr o thir lands, thy hav rtaind thm in communal ownrship, which largly prvails in Württmrg, Badn, Hohnzollrn, and in th Hssian provinc o Starknrg.29 Th communal orsts ar
kpt, as a rul, in an cllnt stat, and in thousands o communs timr and ul wood ar dividd vry yar among all inhaitants; vn th old custom o th Lsholztag is widly sprad: at th ringing o th villag ll all go to th orst to tak as much ul wood as thy can carry.30 In Wstphalia on nds communs in which all th land is cultivatd as on common stat, in accordanc with all rquirmnts o modrn agronomy. As to th old communal customs and haits, thy ar in vigour in most parts o Grmany. Th calling in o aids, which ar ral fêtes o laour, is known to  quit haitual in Wstphalia, Hss, and Nassau. In wlltimrd rgions th timr or a nw hous is usually takn rom th communal orst, and all th nighours join in uilding th hous. Evn in th suurs o Frankort it is a rgular custom among th gardnrs that in cas o on o thm ing ill all com on Sunday to cultivat his gardn.31
      In Grmany, as in Franc, as soon as th rulrs o th popl rpald
thir laws against th pasant associations—that was only in –— ths unions gan to dvlop with a wondrul rapidity, notwithstanding all lgal ostacls which wr put in thir way.32 “It is a act,” Buchnrgr says, “that in thousands o villag communitis, in which no sort o chmical manur or rational oddr was vr known, oth hav com o vryday us, to a quit unorsn tnt, owing to ths associations.” All sorts o laour-saving implmnts and agricultural machinry, and ttr rds o cattl, ar ought through th associations, and various arrangmnts or improving th quality o th produc gin to  introducd. Unions or th sal o agricultural produc ar also ormd, as wll as or prmannt improvmnts o th land.33
      From th point o viw o social conomics all ths forts o th
pasants crtainly ar o littl importanc. Thy cannot sustantially, and still lss prmanntly, allviat th misry to which th tillrs o th soil ar doomd all ovr Europ. But rom th thical point o viw, which w ar now considring, thir importanc cannot  ovrratd.       I might asily multiply such illustrations, taking thm rom Italy,

      Two important conclusions may  drawn rom th ulk o vidnc

      Th Crima and th part o th mainland which lis to th north o it

its annation in , y Grat, Littl, and Whit Russians—Cossacks, rmn, and runaway srs—who cam individually or in small groups rom all cornrs o Russia. Evn pasant propritors who had livd or yars undr th individualist systm rturnd n mass to th communal institutions. Thus, thr is a considral numr o -srs who hav rcivd on-ourth part only o th rgulation allotmnts, ut thy hav rcivd thm r o rdmption and in individual ownrship. Thr was in  a wid-sprad movmnt among thm (in Kursk, Ryazan, Tamov, Orl, tc.) towards putting thir allotmnts togthr and introducing th villag community. Th “r agriculturists” (volnyie khlebopashtsy), who wr liratd rom srdom undr th law o , and had bought thir allotmnts—ach amily sparatly—ar now narly all undr th villag-community systm, which thy hav introducd thmslvs. All ths movmnts ar o rcnt origin, and non-Russians too join thm. Thus th Bulgars in th district o Tiraspol, ar having rmaind or sity yars undr th prsonal-proprty systm, introducd th villag community in th yars –. Th Grman Mnnonits o Brdyansk ought in  or introducing th villag community, and th small pasant propritors (Kleinwirthschaliche) among th Grman Baptists wr agitating in thir villags in th sam dirction. On instanc mor: In th provinc o Samara th Russian govrnmnt cratd in th ortis, y way o primnt,  villags on th systm o individual ownrship. Each houshold rcivd a splndid proprty o  acrs. In , out o th  villags th pasants in  had alrady notid th dsir o introducing th villag community. I tak all ths acts rom th cllnt work o V.V., who simply givs, in a classid orm, th acts rcordd in th aov-mntiond hous-to-hous inqust.
     This movmnt in avour o communal possssion runs adly against
th currnt conomical thoris, according to which intnsiv cultur is incompatil with th villag community. Th acts which w hav or us show, on th contrary, that whrvr th Russian pasants, owing to a concurrnc o avoural circumstancs, ar lss misral than thy ar on th avrag, and whrvr thy nd mn o knowldg and initiativ among thir nighours, th villag community coms th vry mans or introducing various improvmnts in
agricultur and villag li altogthr. Hr, as lswhr, mutual aid is a ttr ladr to progrss than th war o ach against all, as may  sn rom th ollowing acts.
      Undr Nicholas th First’s rul many Crown ocials and sr-own-
rs usd to compl th pasants to introduc th communal cultur o small plots o th villag lands, in ordr to rll th communal storhouss ar loans o grain had n grantd to th poorst commonrs. Such culturs, connctd in th pasants’ minds with th worst rminiscncs o srdom, wr aandond as soon as srdom was aolishd ut now th pasants gin to rintroduc thm on thir own account. In on district (Ostrogozhsk, in Kursk) th initiativ o on prson was sucint to call thm to li in our-hs o all th villags. Th sam is mt with in svral othr localitis. On a givn day th commonrs com out, th richr ons with a plough or a cart and th poorr ons singl-handd, and no attmpt is mad to discriminat on’s shar in th work. Th crop is arwards usd or loans to th poorr commonrs, mostly r grants, or or th orphans and widows, or or th villag church, or or th school, or or rpaying a communal dt.41
      That all sorts o work which ntrs, so to say, in th routin o villag
li (rpair o roads and ridgs, dams, drainag, supply o watr or irrigation, cutting o wood, planting o trs, tc.) ar mad y whol communs, and that land is rntd and madows ar mown y whol communs—th work ing accomplishd y old and young, mn and womn, in th way dscrid y Tolstoi—is only what on may pct rom popl living undr th villag-community systm.42 Thy ar o vryday occurrnc all ovr th country. But th villag community is also y no mans avrs to modrn agricultural improvmnts, whn it can stand th pns, and whn knowldg, hithrto kpt or th rich only, nds its way into th pasant’s hous.
      It has just n said that prctd ploughs rapidly sprad in South

      In th north-ast (Vyatka) small associations o pasants, who travl

     And now, ar having said so much aout mutual aid and support
which ar practicd y th tillrs o th soil in “civilizd” countris, I s that I might ll an octavo volum with illustrations takn rom th li o th hundrds o millions o mn who also liv undr th tutorship o mor

      Th sam applis to our civilizd world. Th natural and social calamitis pass away. Whol populations ar priodically rducd to misry or
